▲ Squad Leader Accused of Colluding with Bandits: Case Transferred to Provincial Authorities

Zhou Lushan, the squad leader, and Chen Gang, the deputy squad leader, of the Dalan Mountain Reconnaissance Squad jointly administered by the governments of Yin, Feng, and Ci counties, were appointed by Wu Conglong, the former commander of the 3rd Regiment of the Security Forces, over a year ago. Recently, the Provincial Security Department received a confidential report alleging that the squad leader and deputy squad leader were suspected of colluding with bandits. The department immediately ordered Yang Zhiqu, the battalion commander of the 2nd Battalion of the 6th Regiment, to arrest them. Upon receiving the order, the battalion commander led soldiers to Dalan Mountain the day before yesterday, disarmed the entire squad, and detained the squad leader and deputy squad leader, Zhou Lushan and Chen Gang, transferring them to the provincial authorities for investigation.

▲ Mother and Son Reunited After Thirty-Nine Years

Li Jiangshi, a resident of Li Hongmao Lane on the north bank of the Yongpu River, is currently 65 years old. She has two sons, the elder named Arong and the younger named Agui. Thirty-nine years ago, on the first day of the eleventh month of the lunar calendar, Li Jiangshi's aunt took Agui to the Sheshijun Temple to watch a play. A sudden fire broke out in the temple, and Agui, then five years old, was separated from his grandmother in the chaos. He was tricked and sold to Zhang Shouchang from Sushan as an adopted son. Zhang owned the Zhengchang Rice Shop at the Dongmenkou in Xiapu County, Fujian Province, and took Agui to Fujian. As he grew older, due to the decline of the family's fortunes, Agui returned to Shao to work as a partner in a tin shop. In February of this year, Agui went to Fujian again to work at Zhao Deli Clock Shop in Zhangzhou. Although Agui traveled back and forth between the two provinces, he always remembered his birth mother. However, he only knew her surname was Li and did not know his father's name or the name of the place where they lived in Yongpu, so he could not come to Yongpu to find his relatives. His mother, Li Jiangshi, had been thinking of Agui very much for thirty years. This spring, she entrusted a relative working in a bank in Xiamen to place a missing person advertisement in a newspaper in Xiamen. In March of this year, the Communists disturbed Zhangzhou, and Agui fled to Xiamen. He unintentionally read the missing person advertisement placed by Li Jiangshi, was overjoyed, and immediately wrote a letter to his birth mother, Li Jiangshi. The day before yesterday, he arrived in Shanghai from Xiamen and took a boat to Yongpu. Upon asking for the house in Li Hongmao Lane and meeting his old mother, they were overcome with grief and joy and embraced each other and cried bitterly. Mother and son have been separated for over thirty-nine years and suddenly reunited, truly a rare and extraordinary event in society.

Education News

Another Setback at National Central University 2

New President Luo Jialun Firmly Declines the Position 3

Students Demand School Opening Without Placement Exams 4

Because the former president refused to take on the difficult task of cleaning up the affairs of the dispersed university, a new president was found. After taking the office, he realized that the job was too difficult and decided to decline the offer, leaving the university without a leader and the students delayed in their studies. Several hundred students, represented by Xu Dehua and four others, took a petition to the Ministry of Education on the morning of the 26th, stating three demands: (1) Determine the opening date of the school as soon as possible to avoid prolonged delay in studies. (2) Change the placement exam to a placement registration, and make up the missed courses from the last semester after the school opens. (If placement exams are held again, first, the previous studies will be erased if the placement exam is failed, which is unacceptable; second, the disturbance was caused by a few students, and the majority should not be hindered by the minority; third, if the placement exam is failed, the grades given by the professors in the past will not be counted, which not only distrusts the professors but also concerns the personality of the faculty and students.) (3) Request the opening of the dormitories (only the second, fourth, and fifth dormitories are currently open; the first and third dormitories, which are more spacious, have not yet been opened) to avoid staying in hotels and facing economic hardship. Senior Secretary Tingzi of the Ministry of Education met with them and stated that the first point would be decided after the president is determined, the second point would be forwarded to the minister for consideration, and the third point was due to the fact that the general affairs section was repairing the dormitories and would be opened after completion. The student representatives, because the president's issue has not been resolved, and the opening of school is still uncertain, went to the Executive Yuan to petition, but did not get what they wanted. It is said that the Ministry of Education has expressed its intention to retain Luo Zhixi and hopes that Luo will reluctantly take on the difficult task, even if he is unwilling to take the position, he should temporarily transition it so that Central University has someone in charge and can prepare for the opening of school as soon as possible. Now some excellent professors at Central University have already taken other positions because Central University is indecisive. Time waits for no one, and September is approaching. Past reorganizations will get on track, and everyone will get rid of the old and start anew, but nothing has been achieved (such as the issues of the president, professors, placement, etc.). It is unknown how to end it well.

The Shanghai Municipal Party Department Sends a Telegram to the Central Government Requesting a Temporary Suspension of Changing the Party Ideology Course to a Civics Course

The National Society stated that recently, the Curriculum Standards Committee of the Ministry of Education decided to change Party Ideology to Civics in primary and secondary schools. The Municipal Party Department believes that now is the time for the opening of schools, and the Civics textbook has not yet been compiled, so it has petitioned the Central Government to temporarily maintain the status quo. The original telegram is recorded below: "Respectfully to the Nanjing Central Executive Committee: According to reports, the Curriculum Standards Committee of the Ministry of Education has decided to change Party Ideology to Civics. Without discussing the merits and demerits, it seems appropriate to maintain the status quo when the Civics curriculum standards have not yet been approved and the Civics textbook has not yet been compiled. Before the new standards are promulgated, the old regulations should be followed. Since some schools have changed Party Ideology to Civics, a special telegram is sent to request the Ministry of Education to issue a notice to all regions to temporarily suspend the change. The Shanghai Special Municipal Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang respectfully asks."

Completion of Reconstruction of School Buildings at Chih Tze College

After the school buildings of the Chih Tze College and its affiliated middle school were burned down by Japanese soldiers, He Shizhen, the principal of the school, devoted himself to rebuilding the college buildings on Shuishui Road. The reconstruction has now been completed, with a brand new appearance and a magnificent view. The details of the school are listed below: "Construction and Equipment" A three-story dormitory can accommodate over a thousand people. A two-story classroom, a large auditorium, an office building, a dining hall, a library, and a sports field have all been completed. New sanitary equipment has been installed. All classrooms and dormitories are equipped with heating pipes. All water and electricity are supplied by the school's own water pump and generator. "Departments and Programs" The original English Department, Political Science Department, and Group A Commerce Department, which were temporarily suspended due to the war last semester, have all been reopened. The Commerce Department has been divided into four groups: Banking, Accounting, International Trade, and Business Administration. The Law Department of the Faculty of Law has been divided into two groups, A and B, due to the large number of students. Group A has classes at the university department on Shuishui Road, while Group B is located in the middle school department and has classes starting at 6:00 PM. The curriculum is the same. Professors for each department have been hired and are all well-known figures in Shanghai. "Affiliated Middle School" The middle school department of the school is still located in the concession. A large building at 56 Hede Road has been rented, and three houses have been rented nearby for use as dormitories. The teaching is in accordance with the original plan. "Enrollment and School Opening" The second round of enrollment for the school has seen a very enthusiastic response. The entrance exams will be held on September 5th and 6th, and the school opening is scheduled for September 12th.

Sports

My Views on "The Future of National Sports" By Wu Yunrui

I read the article "The Future of National Sports" in the August 7th issue of the Ta Kung Pao and understand its main points, which are nothing more than two: first, competitive sports are harmful to health, time-consuming, and costly, implying that they should be abolished; second, local sports save time and money, prevent illness, and prolong life, achieving the purpose of defending the country and managing property. The validity of these conclusions is questionable and I would like to analyze them in detail.

1. The Issue of Competitive Sports Harming Health

In the modern age of scientific development, all conclusions must have a scientific basis, whether based on experiments in natural sciences or statistics in social sciences. Sports belongs to both social and natural sciences, so various issues in sports must be resolved through experimental statistical methods. Those with a little scientific knowledge agree with this. However, the conclusion in the article that "competitive sports are harmful to health" is based on the death of Jin Jianjuan. If this conclusion were credible, then Japan would have completely abolished competitive sports. However, the fact that this has not happened shows that this conclusion is incorrect. The death of Jin Jianjuan was an exceptional case in sports, occupying a position at the extremes of the normal curve in statistics. Statisticians often ignore it, but the reporter of the newspaper used it as a conclusion, revealing a lack of statistical basis. If we take the current situation of sports in Germany as an example to prove it, then it will be even more inappropriate. After the Great War, Germany was restricted by the Allied countries from training soldiers. The government had no choice but to vigorously promote sports, with competitive sports as the main item. Regardless of gender, they received the same training. Every morning and evening, in secluded streets, young men and women were often seen practicing running. If competitive sports really had drawbacks, with Germany's excellent medical science and good equipment, how could it not have been discovered? Therefore, the reporter's statement, The total statistics of national social education in the eighteenth year (1)

The Ministry of Education previously investigated the social education undertakings in the country in the 18th year (from July of the 18th year to June of the 19th year) and has now compiled the statistics. The following is an excerpt from the report.

▲ General Statistics of Various Social Education Undertakings in the Country in the 18th Year

The phrase "examine health" is enough to prove that there is no definite evidence. The physical educators in our country now take the popularization of physical education as a common goal. Does the teaching material used only include competitive sports? Most of those who advocate focusing on competitive sports are a small number of people who do not understand physical education. It is not a disease of physical educators. Among the sports implementation plans passed by the National Sports Conference, there is a section on performance appraisal, the purpose of which is to examine the mass sports achievements of schools and cities, which is to correct the shortcomings of a few people engaged in competition and is in line with the reporter's intention.

2. The Issue of Time Consumption

No country values time more than the United States. An hour of work can earn an average of more than one US dollar. In addition to work time, the rest of the time is used for sports and games to relax the mind. According to the reporter's opinion, isn't this a waste of time? The reason why they reduce working hours and engage in sports and games is that people's energy is limited. The result of one person working continuously for four hours is not as good as the result of someone who takes breaks in between. As society and culture advance, there will be more leisure time, which is natural. In this time of national crisis, all citizens should work hard, which goes without saying. However, the purpose of work is to seek excellent results, and whether the results are good or bad is not directly proportional to the length of working hours, which has long been proven and does not need to be elaborated on. Therefore, to seek excellence in work, it is also necessary to engage in games and sports to regulate mental fatigue and forget the pain of work.

3. The Issue of Economics

Regardless of the type of sports activity, except for gymnastics, the reporter believes that Mr. Liu Changchun's attendance at the World Olympics is solid proof that competitive sports are costly, which is inappropriate. Mr. Liu's attendance this time had a political meaning. If the "Manchukuo" faction dispatched him to attend, it would not be possible. Using a random event as the basis for argument is the same error as hearing of Mr. Jin Jianjuan's death and thinking that sports competitions are harmful to health.

4. Local Sports Prevent Illness and Prolong Life

Modern health education is very developed, and the effect of preventing illness and prolonging life depends on it. Therefore, the art of preventing illness and prolonging life is by no means limited to physical exercise. The reporter's claim to seek national art in local sports is well-founded and seems to have a profound meaning. It is unknown what it is based on. If it is based solely on traditional rhetoric, it may not be credible.

As far as I can see, the future path of national sports will be determined by the following two points:

A. Adapt to Individuality

Individuality is a condition that cannot be ignored in education. Russell advocates this most strongly. The materials used in sports must be suitable for the individuality of children. Our nation has primitive ancestors, who lived in nests and caves, ate raw meat and drank blood. All the instincts of running, jumping, throwing, and chiseling were possessed by our ancestors early on. For thousands of years, they have been deeply rooted in our minds. If you observe elementary school children after school, they gather on the playground and either run or jump. The inheritance of the activities of our ancestors is reappearing in the activities of today's children. What the reporter refers to as foreign sports is actually the remains of the activities of our ancestors. Why do foreigners exist? Because humans are the same, all activities that are in line with their nature are local and not foreign. On the contrary, Swedish gymnastics and German gymnastics do not conform to the nature of children. European and American children abandon them, and our children also hate them deeply. For Europeans and Americans, they are local but also foreign; for us, they are foreign and also foreign. Therefore, it is useless to advocate sports that do not suit the individuality of children, but it is not obedient to prohibit those that do. Foreign sports are foreign, but local sports are also true.

B. Adapt to Society

The life of an individual is entrusted to society. The prosperity and decline, strength and weakness of society are related to the individual. Therefore, the individual must sometimes accommodate society. During the recent Songhu War, the Great Sword Team bravely killed the thieves, and the voice of national art saving the country has since become higher. Its position in sports may be more solid from now on. However, modern international wars rely entirely on science. If the enemy uses planes and artillery to bomb, the great sword will be able to use its skills. Therefore, in order to adapt to the environment and defend the country in the future, we should train soldiers with both intelligence and courage, and cultivate the skills of running, jumping, and climbing. However, this relies on games, ball games, equipment, and track and field sports, which can only be achieved through this. National arts and war are alone.

In the above two points, the former is an economic one and the latter is a balance of rights. In order to be more economical, economic must always be maintained, and the powers can be changed. Abandoning the economic and following the rights will be futile. It is difficult to save time and money. With the author's goal of this or to violate the road and run, compelled by the true righteousness, I dare not be silent. I have made this article to chat for correction.

The 20th Army Volleyball Team Loses to Lingnan

Defeated in Three Consecutive Games

▲ Basketball Battle Tonight

▲ At the China Basketball Hall at 7 PM

The volleyball team of the Sichuan 20th Army Expeditionary Force played a friendly match with the Lingnan volleyball team in this city at the China Athletic Field yesterday afternoon. Although they tried hard, they lost three consecutive games due to slightly inferior skills: 21-14, 21-11, 21-6. The referee was Wei Dingyi.

▲ Fierce Battle in the First Game

The 20th Army served first, but lost points due to excessive force. Lingnan took the lead with 4-1. The guest team resisted with great effort, resulting in a difficult and inseparable situation: 6-6, 7-7. Lingnan won the first half with 11-9, then continued to win with 19-11. The Sichuan Army fought fiercely, but lost the first game with 21-14.

▲ Great Decline in Morale in the Second and Third Games

At the start of the second game, the Sichuan Army adopted a steady approach, trying to slow down the pace. However, they still lost the first half with 11-5 due to the opponent's fierce attack and defensive errors. Lingnan won the second game with 21-11. In the third game, their morale declined further, losing the first half with only three points and a score of 21-6.

▲ Observations on the Guest Team's Skills

The Sichuan Army's performance can be described as follows: (1) Poor teamwork; (2) Uneven talent; (3) Unskilled ball rescue; (4) Many serving errors. The lack of teamwork made it impossible for the offense and defense to be unified. In terms of talent, the center forward and the front row were the most outstanding, but the two flanks and the back row could not provide assistance and rescue, resulting in isolation. The inability to save dangerous balls and the failure to kill the opponent with the ball were also reasons for the defeat. The wind was quite strong yesterday, making it difficult to hit the ball. The Sichuan Army's serve was not accurate and failed to change its tactics according to the wind, resulting in many lost points, which was a pity. Lingnan's performance showed frequent chaotic crowding, which was average. The lineups of the two teams are as follows:

Free Talk

A Branch of the Tanlu Vine Zhan Lu

The "twisting and pulling" in the mouths of Shanghai people, and the "only vines winding around trees, no trees winding around vines" in the mouths of Suzhou people, have now become proverbs. With a puppet state, there must be someone to twist the strings. Muteng went to the puppet state to be the supreme ruler. From then on, every move of the puppet ruler relied on this vine. Motivation: The puppet's silk is tied to the vine branch. If you want to twist the silk, you must pull the vine. This is called twisting and pulling.

China is like a lonely and helpless tree. After a long time, the surrounding branches and leaves are often exploited by the outside world and have no strength to resist. It's okay to just exploit the branches and leaves. Recently, there have been many wild vines that want to bind the tree

On the Attitude of the Great Powers Towards the Japanese Foreign Minister's Speech 7

If Japan truly makes a resolute decision, disregarding all good faith and treaties, then it would be honest to acknowledge this for the sake of the nation. If Japan retains even a slight consideration for good faith and treaties, then regardless of what it does, it will be impossible to justify its actions. If Japan resolutely destroys world peace and willingly disrupts the overall situation in East Asia, then recognizing the puppet state is permissible. Furthermore, advancing to attack Rehe, seize Pingjin, and even disturb the entire nation would also be acceptable. If Japan possesses even a slight concern for safeguarding peace and preserving the overall situation, then regardless of what it does, it will be difficult to justify its actions deviously. The speech given by Foreign Minister Uchida in the Diet stated that recognizing Manchuria is the only method to secure lasting peace in the Far East, that the chaos and revolution within China are the causes of unfortunate changes in international relations in the Far East, that the September 18th Incident was an act of self-defense and did not violate the Kellogg-Briand Pact, that the direct use of force to prevent the infringement of vested interests is a long-standing practice and did not originate with Japan, and that the establishment of the Manchurian state was the result of a separatist movement decided by local leaders, for which Japan bears no responsibility. Finally, he repeatedly declared that Japan has no ambitions for territorial expansion and does not intend to resolve the situation perfunctorily. The various points that contradict the facts are simply too numerous to mention and refute. His words are not only disbelieved by the Chinese people, but also by people from all over the world who are not naive and will not easily believe them. However, the purpose of Foreign Minister Uchida's lengthy statement before the League of Nations report is not to ensure that the great powers will necessarily believe him, but to express his firm and resolute attitude, to reject interference from Britain, the United States, and the League of Nations, to hint subtly at the great powers to see the situation and stop, and to threaten the great powers frankly so that they dare not act rashly. Therefore, the attitude of the great powers towards this statement is worthy of our attention.

According to foreign dispatches, both the British and American governments do not wish to express any opinion on this statement until the investigation team's report is submitted to the League of Nations, temporarily responding to Japan with a closed mouth. This is also because the matter is of great importance, and it is difficult to express an opinion without extremely careful consideration. Although British and American newspapers have mostly criticized and ridiculed the Japanese Foreign Minister's speech, they all conclude that the Japanese have violated the Nine-Power Treaty and the Kellogg-Briand Pact, which cannot be denied. However, we cannot deduce the psychology of the government authorities based on the general public's opinion. The international situation today and diplomatic means are complex and constantly changing, which cannot be predicted by outsiders in advance. What we can assert based on the facts is that the situation in East Asia today has reached a critical and dangerous point, and the calls for a second world war are becoming increasingly urgent. Once a spark ignites, it will immediately erupt. The fuse for this second world war is not in the hands of the Japanese, but in the hands of the British and American powers. The only thing that can sanction those who use force to invade other countries is public justice and righteousness. But it is not enough to sanction with empty words of public justice and righteousness, but only when the majority of powerful nations sincerely believe in this public justice and righteousness can it be sanctioned. If the majority of powerful nations can see that the opportunity cannot be missed, no matter how difficult and arduous, they must work together to maintain this public justice and righteousness. If one or two ambitious people want to use force to destroy our covenant to maintain public justice and righteousness, we should stand up and sanction them, even if they are intimidated, and not be afraid. Then the ambitious people will have to know the difficulty and retreat. Otherwise, if they hesitate and consider using perfunctory reconciliation as a solution, once they are exhausted and the crisis breaks, it will inevitably spread and overflow, and there will be no way to clean it up. Only then will they realize that a temporary peace is not a good plan, but it will be too late. Therefore, I say that those who hold the fuse for the outbreak of disaster today should seriously consider it in advance.

I say this not to borrow the strength of the British and American powers to save ourselves, nor to provoke the great powers to start a war with Japan for my own pleasure. My country is in a situation of military oppression and has long been prepared to be a sacrifice for the world. In today's situation, my country cannot but sacrifice. Even if a world war unfortunately occurs in the future, my country will only be sacrificed. It is a pity that once a war breaks out, it is not only my country that will be sacrificed. All countries in the world will suffer great turmoil. I do not know if the governments of the great powers are willing to abandon the painstaking efforts they have made over the years to promote peace and eliminate war. If not, then at this critical moment, they should have a way to deal with it.

Local News

The "Abolish Civil War Grand Alliance" Was Established, Representative Conference Held Yesterday 9

▲ 449 representatives from various provinces and cities attended

▲ Public announcement declaring the establishment yesterday

▲ Proposal review meeting held at 2 PM

▲ Meeting continues this morning to discuss proposals

The Abolish Civil War Grand Alliance held a representative conference at the City Chamber of Commerce at 9 AM yesterday, officially establishing the alliance. 371 representatives from various provincial and municipal groups and 78 individual members attended. In the morning, the presidium and proposal review committee were elected, and the declaration of establishment was passed. The proposal review committee organized the proposals in the afternoon, and the conference will continue this morning. The details are recorded separately below.

Opening Ceremony Yesterday Morning 10

▲ Venue Arrangement: The Abolish Civil War Grand Alliance representative conference was held in the City Chamber of Commerce auditorium. A cloth banner with the name of the alliance was hung at the entrance, and Boy Scouts maintained order. Those without badges were not allowed to enter. The badges were in four colors: red for the presidium, yellow for group representatives, pink for individual members, and white for staff. National flags were hung in the four corners of the venue, and slogans such as "Never Cooperate with Those Who Engage in Civil War" and "Abolishing Civil War is the Way to Find a Way Out for the Chinese Nation" were displayed. The atmosphere was very solemn. The seats were all marked with numbers, and attendees had to match their attendance certificate numbers to their seats in order, and the order was well maintained.

▲ Conference Staff: Presidium: Wang Xiaolai, Wu Daquan, Liu Zhan'en (the above three were nominated by the preparatory committee), Lin Kanghou, Chen Shucheng (Principal of Wuchang China University), Yang Meizhen (Deputy Executive Director of the Women's Temperance Society), Lu Zhangyuan (Guangdong Member). Secretary Director: Yan Esheng. Secretaries: Tao Leqin, Wu Zhongyi, Gu Huaibing. Master of Ceremonies: Ge Tianhao.

▲ Conference Proceedings: The meeting was announced to begin at 9 AM. Wang Xiaolai, the interim chairman, conducted the ceremony as usual. (1) Election of the Presidium. Wang Xiaolai reported first. The Presidium was stipulated to have seven members. Three had already been nominated by the preparatory committee. The remaining four were to be publicly elected by the conference. Xu Jiqian proposed the distribution of the four members, with the National Federation of Commerce, the women's sector, Wuhan, and Guangdong each occupying one member. Dai Tianqiu proposed that the Presidium nominate candidates according to the above criteria. There was no dissent, and the Presidium nominated Lin Kanghou, Yang Meizhen, Chen Shucheng, and Lu Zhangyuan. There was no dissent, and they were approved. (2) Chairman Wu Daquan delivered the opening speech (recorded separately). (3) Chairman Lin Kanghou reported on the preparatory process (recorded separately). (4) Chairman Yang Meizhen had Secretary Director Yan Esheng read the declaration of establishment drafted by the preparatory committee, which was then voted on and passed. The original declaration is recorded separately. (5) Organization of the Proposal Review Committee. Chairman Wu Daquan explained that the Presidium would nominate candidates for the review committee and seek the consent of the conference. Dai Tianqiu objected to the review committee arbitrarily picking and choosing, which would erase the original proposers' intentions. The chairman explained that it was only for organizing and merging to facilitate discussion. The chairman then nominated 29 people, read out the list, and it was passed without dissent (list recorded separately). (6) Photography. (7) Representatives' Speeches. The chairman explained that each person should not exceed ten minutes. Afterwards, Huang Wenzhong and 13 others spoke in turn (the main points of the speeches are recorded separately). The meeting was then adjourned, and the City Chamber of Commerce hosted lunch. ▲ Formation of the Review Committee: The preparatory committee received many proposals to abolish civil war. In addition to the 55 items received earlier, which were included in the special issue compiled and printed by the National Federation of Commerce, more than 20 items were received later. Each proposal included many aspects of the problem, and repetition was inevitable. Discussing each item would not only be short on time but also not necessary in fact. The conference specially elected Wang Xiaolai, Wu Daquan, Liu Zhan'en, Lin Kanghou, Chen Shucheng, Yang Meizhen, Lu Zhangyuan (the above seven members of the Presidium are ex officio members), Zhu Xuefan, Li Kuian, Xu Jiqian, Wang Yunwu, Hu Xisheng, Lu Xiaobo, Wen Lanting, Chen Zheqing, Qian Xinzhi, Yu Xiaochuan, Yu Rongqiao, Quan Runquan, Chen Yafu, Li Zushen, Qin Qiqing, Yong Jianqiu, Wu Hexuan, Wang Yansong, Chen Liting, Lao Jingxiu, Pu Xinya, Zhou Xuexiang, and 29 other people to form the Proposal Review Committee, which met at the Bank Club at 2 PM to organize the proposals.

Declaration Announcing Establishment 11

The Abolish Civil War Grand Alliance issued a declaration of establishment yesterday, saying: "To the gentlemen of all circles in the country: We, the undersigned, in view of the severity of internal and external troubles, have initiated the Abolish Civil War Grand Alliance in order to secure domestic peace and confront foreign aggression. As of today, those who support the charter of this association and have joined as initiators total 401 groups and 1,057 individuals. Geographically, they cover more than 20 provinces and major overseas cities. Professionally, they cover agriculture, industry, commerce, and education. We hereby solemnly declare the establishment of the Abolish Civil War Grand Alliance at a representative conference in Shanghai today. We hereby notify you by telegram. The Abolish Civil War Grand Alliance."

Compilation of Speeches and Reports 12

▲ Chairman's Speech: Chairman Wu Daquan delivered the opening speech, saying: "Gentlemen, today we are holding the representative conference of the Abolish Civil War Grand Alliance. We are grateful that representatives from various provinces and cities have arrived as scheduled, and many have come from afar despite the heat. The four groups that initially initiated this conference in Shanghai are extremely grateful. I am entrusted by the preparatory committee to explain the purpose of the conference to you, which is also a great honor. Gentlemen, what has China come to today? The enemy has occupied the land and people of our three provinces with a small number of troops, and there is nothing we can do. They have devastated our major commercial ports, taking numerous lives and destroying property, and there is nothing we can do. The situation in Rehe and Yubian is alarming again, and the scope of aggression is expanding without end. China, with its vast land, rich resources, and large population, is being trampled upon to this extent. We are truly heartbroken and tearful when we think about it. The reason for this is mostly due to the continuous civil wars of the past 20 years, which have only destroyed the country's wealth and the people's strength, resulting in weakness and stagnation, inviting this great foreign humiliation. This is an extremely clear fact, and there is no need to deny or doubt it. So we can see that everyone understands that the survival of our country and nation can only be achieved through unity against foreign aggression, by taking the path of long-term resistance. We now understand even more that to resist the enemy in the long term, we must first take the path of abolishing civil war. This is what everyone in the country has felt in their conscience since the September 18th Incident, and it is also the motive for the initiation of this conference. I am sure that everyone present here shares this sentiment, and I will not elaborate further. However, there are about three points that I would like to explain to you about the points to pay attention to in this movement. (1) This movement of ours is a universal movement of the people. Regardless of individual, group, gender, occupation, or party affiliation, we hope that they will join in order to have a great and rapid effect. The types of members need to be universal, so the goals of the movement must be as simple as possible. Anyone who agrees with the abolition of civil war can join this conference and work together on this common goal. Other differences in personal opinions and behaviors are not what this conference intends to ask about. Therefore, the charter of this conference stipulates, "This conference shall not engage in any other activities other than the movement to abolish civil war." The intention of this article is not to oppose other movements. There are many kinds of movements that are needed to eliminate the root causes of civil war, and this conference is well aware of this, and earnestly hopes that the members of this conference will gather together with those who share the same purpose to carry out various individual movements to assist or promote the success of this conference. However, in a movement of this conference with the commonality of the general public, it is necessary to set a simple and clear scope in order to avoid differences of opinion. Therefore, the charter also stipulates that "The movement of this conference to abolish civil war shall be carried out in the following order: (A) In peacetime, this conference shall issue public texts or speeches, stating the evils of civil war and explaining the benefits of peace. (B) If political disputes arise that are sufficient to cause civil war, this conference shall advise both parties to trust a certain public opinion organ (before a formal national representative organ is established, a statutory non-governmental professional body can replace it) to mediate, and neither party shall absolutely resolve it by force. (C) If civil war unfortunately occurs, the group members and individual members of this conference shall unanimously refuse to cooperate and shall adopt peaceful and appropriate methods to stop it." This is what I hope everyone in this conference will pay attention to. (2) This movement organ should not exist in countries where politics has long been stable, because there is no need for it to exist. Therefore, although we have initiated this conference, we really hope that this movement will be successful as soon as possible and that this organ will disappear as soon as possible. Therefore, the charter stipulates that "The term of this conference shall be temporarily set at five years, but if no civil war occurs before the expiration date, and it is considered unnecessary to carry out the movement to abolish it again, it may be dissolved in advance." It can be seen that the members of this conference do not want to make use of this organ. But if civil war cannot be eliminated, we are prepared to fight to the end. This is what I hope everyone in this conference will pay attention to. (3) The abolish war movement is a peace movement. Since we take peace as our purpose, our movement method is of course to adopt peaceful methods. Therefore, the charter stipulates that when it is absolutely necessary, we will adopt the principle of non-cooperation, and everyone should strictly restrain themselves. But we believe that this principle can be thoroughly implemented or even more effective than any other principle. This is what I hope everyone in this conference will pay attention to. Finally, I can clearly state to you that I believe that if we follow the spirit of the charter of this conference, set up more branches, recruit more members, and everyone strives for this simple goal, civil war can absolutely be eliminated, and therefore foreign insults can absolutely be resisted. I hereby wish the success of this conference in advance."

▲ Preparatory Report: Chairman Lin Kanghou reported on the preparatory process on behalf of the preparatory committee, saying: (1) The motivation for preparation: More than 20 years have passed since the establishment of the Republic of China, and the method used to solve national affairs has always been to resort to force. So far, where are all the rights of freedom and equality? Which is better and which is worse is self-evident. We often think about which is better between force and peace. Now, after 20 years of trial, we have proved the wrong of force. However, some people doubt that we have no weapons in our hands, and what ability do we have to abolish civil war? It is unknown that organization can generate power. Foreigners often say that Chinese people are a plate of loose sand, with no organizational ability. The initiation of the Abolish Civil War Grand Alliance is the best test of whether Chinese people have organizational ability. Since its publication, it has had a great impact in various places, which shows that abolishing civil war is what everyone wants. Whoever has this reason in common. (2) Preparatory process: A) From the initiation to the present, it has been four months, and the preparatory committee was established on June 30th. Up to August 26th, a total of 16 preparatory meetings were held. (B) As of yesterday, a total of 401 groups and 1,057 individuals have joined the initiators, including 8 commercial association federations, 72 commercial associations in various cities and counties, 10 banking associations, 9 financial associations, 104 industry associations, 42 industry associations, 18 overseas Chinese groups, 11 women's groups, 11 hometown groups, 59 academic groups, and 58 other groups. (C) Calculated by province, there are Hebei, Shandong, Shanxi, Henan, Shaanxi, Gansu, Sichuan, Yunnan, Guizhou, Hubei, Hunan, Jiangxi, Anhui, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Fujian, Guangdong, Guangxi, Suiyuan, Jilin, and other provinces, as well as Zhangjiakou, Weihaiwei, Qingdao, Beiping, Tianjin, Taiyuan, Nanjing, Guangzhou, Shanghai, a total of 29 provinces and cities, and overseas Chinese in Vietnam, Singapore, Batavia, Maipo, Hong Kong, Macau, Myanmar, etc. It can be said that a plate of loose sand has been glued together. (D) As of 7:30 pm on the 26th, 355 group representatives and 77 individual members had registered, totaling 432 people. This morning, 16 group representatives and 1 individual member from afar continued to arrive, totaling 449 people. (3) A glimpse of the preparation period: When Chen Jitang and Chen Ce of Guangdong clashed, the preparatory committee sent Mr. Zhu Ziqiao, Chen Liting, and Zha Liangzhao to Guangdong to persuade them. At the beginning, the Guangdong side was quite suspicious of what background our association had. After a detailed explanation, they frankly believed it. Although we dare not say that the early resolution of this clash between the two Chens was due to the efforts of the three representatives of our association, the three representatives were actually able to resolve it so quickly. After the official establishment of this association, the responsibility for eliminating civil war is even heavier, and the method of its work can be summed up in one word: "begging bitterly." This is what Chairman Wu said about adopting peaceful means.

▲ Representatives' Speeches: (1) Huang Wenzhong said that there are many representatives present today, but there are very few who actually come from the fields. There may even be no farmers who actually farm the land, which is a bit disappointing. In Gansu Province, the number of people who have died directly or indirectly from civil war in recent years has reached more than 3 million, which is about the same as the population of Shanghai. However, due to inconvenient transportation, no one pays attention. Recently, although some people have advocated developing the Northwest because of the fall of the Northeast, if civil war breaks out again, there will be no way to do it. In the future, we must arouse the people, make a great determination, and fight to the end with the soldiers who initiate civil war. Otherwise, relying only on passive non-cooperation, under the threat of guns, we will have to cooperate with pain. There are many meetings and speeches in the treaty ports, but it is feared that organizing abolish war branches in the inland provinces will lead to unwarranted disasters. He also cited the example of the rise of European and Asian countries after World War I. (3) Hu Jianru, representative of the Nanchang City Education Association, said briefly that Jiangxi has suffered from the scourge of the Communist Party since the 18th year of the Republic of China. China has fought a total of 32 wars from the Second Revolution to the clash between the two Chens in Guangdong. At that time, there was no public criticism. Today, representatives from all provinces and cities in the country have come here to discuss the abolition of civil war, which can be said to be a turning point for the revival of the Chinese nation. ▲Proposals in Preparation, the proposals of the Preparatory Committee, after review by the Proposal Review Committee, are listed as the first category of proposals. They will be discussed first during the Second Delegates' Congress today. The original proposals are as follows: (1) Each province and city should quickly borrow houses from chambers of commerce or other institutions to set up branches, and the Standing Committee should quickly formulate the articles of association and contact them for handling; (2) The head office and branches in each province and city should quickly publish advertisements in newspapers and send people to solicit members. All organizations and individuals who have joined the initiators should also be introduced to members separately and quickly; (3) According to Article 2, Item 1 of the articles of association, the head office should quickly issue a periodical "Abolish Civil War" and send it to the branches in each province and city on a regular basis. In the location of the head office and branches, famous people should be hired to give public speeches on "Abolish Civil War" at any time; (4) According to Article 3, Item 2 of the articles of association, personnel of the head office and branches should investigate at any time whether there are political disputes in various places that may cause civil war, report to the Standing Committee, and try to prevent them; (5) According to the provisions of Article 3, Item 2 of the articles of association, the Standing Committee should select the proposals of each member, study methods to peacefully stop the outbreak of civil war, and designate members familiar with the situation in various places and industries as commissioners to study separately for temporary adoption by the Standing Committee; (6) The head office's expenses, according to Article 8 of the articles of association, are planned to be raised through donations from joining organizations and individuals. Each organization is free to determine the amount of annual donation from 50 to 500 yuan, and each individual is free to determine the amount of annual donation from 5 to 100 yuan. If the above donations are not enough for the use of this association, donations may be raised from organizations and individuals outside the association to supplement it.

Eurasia Aviation Will Open Next Month, Test Flight Plane in Lanzhou 17

▲Shanghai to Xinjiang Ticket Price Needs More Than 1,500 Yuan

▲Beijing-Shanghai Line Can Resume Original Flight on the 6th of Next Month

▲Guangzhou-Hankou Line is Being Actively Planned

Eurasia Aviation, since Li Jingcong, the former director of the Eurasia Aviation Company's management team, made a test flight last year with good results.

Page 18

The company actively prepared for it. After several board meetings, it was decided that August and September would be the full-line test flight time. The company immediately followed the resolution and sent Liao Guanxuan, the director of the Operations Team, and Shi Mide, the director of the Aviation Team, by plane from Beiping on the 10th of this month to conduct a full-line test flight. According to Mr. Sun Mutang, the company's secretary, the test flight process, the exact date of the official opening, and the planning situation of the Guangzhou-Hankou line are quite detailed, and are recorded as follows:

▲Test Flight Plane Stays in Lanzhou According to Mr. Sun, the Eurasia airline, since Liao Guanxuan, the director of the Operations Team of this company, and Shi Mide, the director of the Aviation Team, took the Eurasia No. 6 plane and took off from Beiping, arrived in Lanzhou earlier. Due to the arrangement of stations along the way and the problem of gasoline, there were many delays on the way. In addition, due to the climate of Suzhou, it is still staying in Lanzhou. The report said that it had been test-flying from Lanzhou to Dihua, and it was said that the industry had flown back from Dihua, and the test flight was successful. All were not facts. This company still received a telegram from Shi Mide yesterday, and it is indeed in Lanzhou. It will continue to fly within days. The arrangement between the stations that passed by is almost ready, and there is no problem with gasoline. However, in the future official flight, the gasoline from Hami to Dihua will still need to be purchased from Russia. Although there is gasoline in Xinjiang, it has not been refined and cannot be used. After the success of transportation in the future, after the development is implemented there, the gasoline problem seems not to have to be purchased from Russia again. As for the section from Hami to Dihua, this section is the most difficult place to fly on the entire line. The middle of the road is all desert, and it takes seven days for daily transportation, which is carried by camels. If the test flight is successful in the future, transportation will be much easier.

▲Ticket Price and Time The test flight plane has decided to complete the full line back to Shanghai within a week. It is expected to officially open to traffic around the 15th of next month. As for the time and ticket price, it is currently being drafted. The approximate full-line ticket price is about 1,500 yuan. It is estimated that it will be 50 yuan from Shanghai to Nanjing, 100 yuan from Nanjing to Luoyang, 75 yuan from Luoyang to Xi'an, 230 yuan from Xi'an to Lanzhou, 300 yuan from Lanzhou to Suzhou, 270 yuan from Suzhou to Hami, 250 yuan from Hami to Dihua, and 275 yuan from Dihua to Tacheng.

▲Beijing-Shanghai Route Also, the line from Shanghai to Nanjing was temporarily suspended due to the impact of the January 28th Shanghai Incident. Since the ceasefire, passengers on the Beijing-Shanghai line have felt inconvenient. Therefore, this company is still actively preparing to resume it. It is expected that it will be able to resume flights around the 6th of next month.

▲Guangzhou-Hankou Route As for the Guangzhou-Hankou route, it starts from Guangzhou, passes through Changsha, and goes to Hankou. This company had wanted to plan to open it earlier, so that it could be connected to the Xi'an section of the Eurasia Line. It can also be said to be a branch line of the Eurasia Aviation. It is still being actively planned and will definitely be realized in the future. After the Eurasia route is completed, there will be the Pingluo line in the north and the Guangzhou-Hankou line in the south, which can collect postal items from the north and south and transport them to the Eurasia main line, directly connecting to Europe.

Shanghai Banks Prepaid Paper Money Tax Yesterday 18

▲Collected by the Central Bank on behalf of the government, the tax rate is reduced

▲Foreign banks are negotiating for collection

▲The Ministry of Finance agrees to reduce the tax rate by 1.2%

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, as a result of repeated consultations between the representatives of the Bankers Association and Finance Minister Song, the Ministry of Finance has agreed to reduce the tax rate. However, the exact amount of the reduction must be formally announced after being reviewed by the Ministry of Finance. However, because the Ministry of Finance is in urgent need of funds, it first asked the issuing banks to prepay the tax. It is heard that by yesterday, all domestic issuing banks in this city had paid the tax, which was sent to the Central Bank for collection on their behalf. The foreign banks that issue banknotes include HSBC, Standard Chartered, Citibank, Oriental, and Banque Sino-Belge, etc. The total amount of issuance is also considerable. It is heard that the government is negotiating for collection.

According to the Central News Agency, the issue of the Ministry of Finance's collection of the paper money issuance tax has been discussed repeatedly. The other day, the banking representatives Li Fusun and Hu Bijiang visited Minister Song again to continue discussions. According to the Central News Agency reporter, the reasons for the Ministry of Finance's collection of the paper money issuance tax this time are two: (1) The issuers of banknotes in all countries are national banks. Although various different banknotes can be circulated in one country, the right to issue them all belongs to the government, just like our country's stamps. Although there are various different stamps such as Sun Yat-sen, Liao Zhongkai, and Huang Xing, the right to issue them all belongs to the government. Our country's banknotes are not like that. Commercial banks can also issue them with special permission. According to statistics, the total amount of banknotes currently circulating in the country is about 300 million yuan, and those issued by commercial banks account for the majority of them. In order to prevent banknotes from flooding the market, the government has decided to implement the collection of the paper money issuance tax based on the principle that the right to issue banknotes belongs to the government. (2) In order to maintain the government's credit, Minister Song has tried to pay the principal and interest of the government bonds of 8 million yuan per month on schedule, no matter how difficult the finances are. The monthly expenditure on military and political expenses is also very large. Therefore, it is necessary to seek new sources of income. The collection of the paper money issuance tax was promulgated by the Central Government a long time ago. Therefore, the Ministry of Finance has decided to implement the collection in accordance with the order and will never stop it due to any difficulties. This time, the banking sector requested the Ministry of Finance to reduce the tax rate due to the economic downturn. The Ministry of Finance has agreed to reduce it slightly. However, the banking sector requested that it be reduced to 1%, because it is too different from the original tax rate, and it is difficult to make it a reality. The minimum limit of the Ministry of Finance is to reduce it to 1.5%. As for the matter of borrowing money from the banking sector, the Ministry of Finance strongly denied it. Minister Song has decided to fly to Beijing today, but this issue will not be stopped because Song has left Shanghai. Since the Ministry of Finance has agreed to reduce the tax rate, the intermediary will come out to mediate in order to find a solution.

Song and Cai Fly to Beijing Today 19

According to the Central News Agency, Song Ziwen, the Vice President of the Executive Yuan and concurrently the Minister of Finance, has been in Shanghai to negotiate financial issues for many days. The Central Government has repeatedly urged him to return to Beijing to act as the President of the Executive Yuan. Chiang Kai-shek also telegraphed Song the night before last to urge him. It is now learned that Song has decided to fly to Beijing with Cai Tingkai, the Commander-in-Chief of the 19th Route Army, today. Cai is going to report to the Central Government on the recent situation of suppressing bandits in Fujian Province. According to Xin Sheng News Agency, Song Ziwen, the acting President of the Executive Yuan, had planned to go to Beijing the day before yesterday, but he could not make it because the matters he was handling in Shanghai were not completed. It is now learned that Song has decided to go to Beijing today or tomorrow. Before leaving Shanghai, Song had many pending cases regarding the blockade of the customs. Yesterday morning at about 10:00, he summoned Zhang Fuyun, the Director of the Customs Administration, to his residence for a meeting. The conversation lasted for one and a half hours before Director Zhang left. Mayor Wu Tiecheng also visited Song yesterday.

Hongkou Organizations Sent Representatives to Petition the Municipal Government 20

▲Negotiations on the Activities of Japanese Rogues

The Shanghai Citizens' Federation, the Hongkou District Branches, and the Joint Office of the Commercial Federation of Hanbil Road, Jiaxing Road, Tongzhou Road, Yangshupu Road, Broadway Road, Wuchang Road, Haining Road, East and West Huade Road, Yinxiang Road, Suzhou Road, Algin Road, Chuanbao Road, North Xizang Road, North Jiangxi Road, and other organizations, according to the resolutions of yesterday's emergency meeting, elected representatives to submit a petition to the Municipal Government, requesting negotiations to ban the activities of Japanese rogues in the Hongkou area, and demanding compensation for the damage caused by the Japanese Marines to the Chen Wanxing Factory on Washington Road and Yangzhou Road, and for the stabbing of Chinese people. The representatives are scheduled to petition the Municipal Government before the 29th. The text of the petition is attached below:

The petition is to request your government to make serious protests in order to maintain peace and tranquility among the people, due to the armed arrogance of the Japanese police team and the red-shirt group in the Hongkou area, which has created a dangerous situation. Since the January 28th Shanghai Incident, the citizens of Hongkou have suffered greatly. Each returned to their respective places, hoping to survive the disaster and restore the market. However, the Japanese ambition and cunning are that the troop withdrawal was not long before the Marines armed and ferocious, and came to violence again. At 11:00 pm on the 10th of this month, they went to Washington Road, Yangzhou Road and other places, and were demolishing the bamboo fences of the Chen Wanxing factory, and stabbing many Chinese people (the details have been presented before), causing the citizens of this district to be panicked all day long. Moreover, this district is under the jurisdiction of the Public Concession police power. Any accident that occurs is responsible for maintaining local security. Now, Japanese rogues have organized the Japanese Police Team and the Red-Shirt Group, citing the Asian Company bombing case, and divided them into reconnaissance patrol and protection teams, each team of 20 people, rampant in various districts, causing great panic among the citizens. The usually peaceful market has suddenly become a terrifying and dangerous environment. Shanghai has suffered a violent change, and the commercial depression has been unbearable to recover. How can the Japanese act recklessly for no reason, causing the local area to present a disturbing atmosphere, and businessmen and people cannot live and work in peace, and feel even more painful. The associations held a joint meeting of representatives from various districts on the 26th of this month, and resolved to send representatives to petition the Municipal Government, quickly put forward serious negotiations, stop the Japanese rogues from acting recklessly, in order to maintain commerce and stabilize the locality, etc. The reason is to submit a document by Zhang Xianfang, Wang Rongtang, and other six representatives to submit to your government, petition for everything, to hope to see, and to negotiate according to reason, and must achieve the goal, in order to save the citizens of Hongkou into a stable environment, then the recovery of industry and commerce, depends on this move, respectfully present.

Japanese Soldiers Visited Zhabei Again Yesterday 21

▲Praying at the Japanese Cemetery for the Fallen Japanese Soldiers

According to Datong News Agency, the new Marine Corps soldiers who came to Shanghai from Japan yesterday morning at 9:00 continued to visit the Zhabei war zone. The Public Security Bureau of the Five Districts, in order to comply with the order of the Municipal Government, sent police to guide them to avoid misunderstandings among the citizens. Therefore, police chief Wang Molin led four policemen on bicycles to wait at the intersection of North Sichuan Road and Hongjiang Road in advance. When the Marine Corps arrived, they joined forces to guide them to visit the war zones. The route they took was the same as yesterday. Only when they finally arrived at Yokohama Road, all the Marine Corps soldiers got off the bus and entered the Japanese Cemetery to silently pray in front of the tombs of the fallen Japanese soldiers in the Shanghai War buried there. After five minutes, they came out and divided into two columns, one from Tiantong'an Station and the other from East Yokohama Road Dourui An Road to return. Yesterday, Navy Major Koyoshi Yoshihiro and another military officer-like person led the team, riding in two cars, and seven other trucks were loaded with the new Marine Corps soldiers coming and going. There was also a motorcycle, and the rider seemed to be the company commander. The number of people was still 150. The visit lasted from 9:00 to 10:15.

Since the January 28th Incident, national product factories have been destroyed. At this time of commercial depression and market recession, the future of national products is extremely dangerous. Our people should uphold the heart of self-love and patriotism, and strive to formulate methods of resistance, and implement self-production, self-manufacture and self-use.

If so, national products can be developed, and the source will not flow out, and the economic invasion methods of those generations will have no way to achieve. The British public bus strike, because the company refused the workers' demands, the two sides went to extremes, resulting in many disturbances. Yesterday, an incident of pouring hydrochloric acid on the bus occurred, and the situation is getting worse. The details are recorded as follows:

The bus body immediately caught fire. The clothes of four passengers were all burned. A passenger in his 30s

The passenger, in an attempt to escape, jumped out of the bus and injured his head. He was later sent to Tongren Hospital by the police who rushed to treat him. At 6:20, Route 9 bus was also thrown ammunition by workers at the intersection of Tongfu Road and Jing'an Temple Road, injuring two passengers. At 6:40, when Route 10 bus was driving on North Nichengqiao, someone threw hydrochloric acid ammunition, and the car caught fire. Passengers Jin Abao and Li Heshang were injured. The police station sent a large number of detectives to hunt down the murderer, but he had escaped. At the same time, the company heard the news and immediately rushed to the scene of the accident for inspection by deputy manager Pia (transliteration), and then returned to the company to report.

▲Removing White Russians After the Chinese workers went on strike, the company hired more than 40 White Russians to maintain business, serving as ticket sellers. However, because of the language barrier, disputes often occurred with passengers, and it was discovered that there was also embezzlement. American Sailor Drunk and Beats a Chinese Man to Death 30

▲ Four Sailors Dancing and Drinking

▲ Forcibly Taking Fruit from a Vendor

▲ Eating It All Without Paying a Cent

▲ Vendor Beaten and Dies from Injuries

At the dance hall of the Jue Lu Hotel on Xizang Road, at 10:30 PM on the 25th, four American naval soldiers stationed in Shanghai, not wearing uniforms, arrived. They danced and drank to their heart's content before leaving. When they left the venue, they were all drunk and staggering. Passing by a fruit vendor, Wu Da Kui from Changzhou, on the side of the road across from the Jue Lu Hotel, they each grabbed the fruits from Wu's basket and devoured them. In a short while, they emptied the basket without paying a single penny and left. Wu hurriedly demanded payment from them, but the four sailors became enraged due to their drunkenness. They suddenly punched Wu with their fists. One of the sailors even used the stool Wu was sitting on to beat Wu's head and other parts of his body. Wu was outnumbered and, as it was late at night, could not call for help. Although a few passersby saw the injustice, none dared to offer assistance. As a result, Wu was severely beaten and fell to the ground in pain. The sailors were about to flee when, fortunately, nearby patrol officers heard the alarm and arrived, taking both parties to the Old Zhabei Police Station. After questioning by the police chief, Wu was ordered to be sent to Renji Hospital for treatment, and the four sailors were handed over to their officers for investigation. However, Wu's injuries were very serious, and he was already forty-two years old. He died the next morning. The hospital then informed the police station to send the body to the Philen Road autopsy center in Hongkou. They also began investigating the family members of the deceased. After a day of effort, they only found Zhu Su Lin, a relative of the deceased. The family members were all in their hometown. At 10:00 AM yesterday, the police station sent Zhu and witnesses Wu Fu'an and Zhou Bosheng, who had seen the assault, to the autopsy center. Subsequently, Guo Wei, a prosecutor from the First Special District Local Court, along with a clerk and a forensic doctor, arrived at the center to conduct an autopsy. After the examination, they took their seats in public. The Western police chief reported the occurrence and investigation of the case and presented the autopsy report. However, none of the four sailors were present. According to the testimony of Wu and Zhou, they were passing by at the time and witnessed the brutal assault. The four sailors were not wearing uniforms but were dressed in ordinary Western suits and pants, all in the same yellow color. The assailant who used the stool had a red tie. As for the person's build, it was of medium height and well-proportioned, neither too fat nor too thin, with no special features. If they saw him again, they would still be able to identify him, they said. After Guo, the prosecutor, completed the autopsy and interrogation, he ordered Zhu Su Lin to sign a bond and claim the body for coffin burial.

Songbao Long-Distance Bus 31

▲ Scheduled to Start Service on September 1st

The Wusong City Songyang Long-Distance Bus Company suffered extensive damage to its vehicles during the recent war, resulting in significant losses. Unable to resume operations, it has been suspended until now. Reactions to the National Movement Committee's Telegram 32

Since the Central Party Headquarters' Mass Movement Guidance Committee issued a telegram regarding the issue of enterprises, it has attracted the attention of various industrial groups and domestic goods factories across the country. They have jointly issued a declaration and submitted it to the Central Party Headquarters and various ministries and departments, requesting a correction. The original text is reproduced below:

▲ Declaration: Yesterday, we read in the newspapers that, regarding the labor-capital dispute at the Shanghai Sanyou Industrial Society, the Central Party Headquarters' Mass Movement Guidance Committee, in its telegram to the Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters and the Municipal Government, stated that "extraordinary means should be used to force the capitalists to resume work by a specific date." Article 37 of the Provisional Constitution states that the people have the freedom to engage in business. In law, this is an absolute private right. Forcing work to resume is not only a violation of the spirit of the Provisional Constitution but also sets a bad precedent unprecedented in the world. China's industry is just beginning to sprout. In the past four or five years, the government has repeatedly issued orders and declarations to protect it. Now, the facts are quite the opposite, and we are even more apprehensive. We dare to express our sincere opinions and seek the protection of public opinion to achieve a legal and proper solution. We hereby make this solemn declaration and respectfully hope that all sectors will take note. Yong'an Textile Company, Yixin Toothbrush Factory, Dalong Iron Factory, Dacheng Textile Factory, Dasheng Yarn Factory, Great China Match Co., Ltd., Tianzhang Paper Factory, Wuzhou Gubeng Factory, Wuhe Weaving Factory, Zhonghua Iron Factory, China Ya'pu'er Electric Appliance Factory, China Enamel Factory, China Chemical Industry Society, Minfeng Yarn Factory, Oriental Nianhong Electric Light Company, Zhentai Yarn Factory, Mei Ya Silk Weaving Factory, Taishan Brick and Tile Company, Yaguang Optical Manufacturing Company, Puyi Yarn Factory, Kangyuan Factory, Zhanghua Woolen Textile Co., Ltd., Dafeng Dyeing and Weaving Factory, Huasheng Electric Appliance Manufacturing Factory, Huafu Hat Factory, Kaicheng Acid Manufacturing Factory, Guochang Enamelware Sales Office, Hongzhang Textile Company, Shixing Yarn Factory, Sulun Yarn Factory, Lingsheng Ink Co., Ltd., Sanxin Dyeing and Weaving Factory, Hongxin Dyeing and Weaving Factory, Yingzhou Dyeing and Weaving Factory, Tianyuan Electrochemical Factory, Tianchu Monosodium Glutamate Factory, Jiangnan Paper Mill, Yuanyuan Weaving Company, Great China Rubber Factory, Yonghe Industrial Company Baoxing Steel Refining Factory, Shengde Weaving Factory, Zhenhua Paint Company, China Industrial Factory, China Merchant Shanghai Cement Company, Qiming Dyeing and Weaving Factory, Qinfeng Dyeing and Weaving Factory, Guanshengyuan Co., Ltd.

▲ Telegram to the Central Party Headquarters in Nanjing, the National Government, and various ministries and departments: We have read in the newspapers that the Central Party Headquarters' Mass Movement Guidance Committee, in its telegram to the Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters and the Municipal Government regarding the labor-capital dispute at the Sanyou Industrial Society, stated that "extraordinary means should be used to force the capitalists to resume work by a specific date." According to Article 37 of the Provisional Constitution, the people have the freedom to engage in business. In law, this is an absolute private right and is not subject to public law. Now, the words in the telegram order that extraordinary means be used to force work to resume. It should be considered whether these steps are consistent with the Provisional Constitution. The Provisional Constitution only explicitly states that businesses that violate the law should be ordered to close. We have not heard of any regulations that force work to resume. If such a precedent is set, not only will the people's freedom to engage in business be unable to be guaranteed, but the country's credit will also lose its dignity. China's industry is just beginning to sprout. It is subjected to the economic pressure of the great powers externally and the pain of natural disasters and man-made calamities internally. Maintaining the status quo is already extremely difficult. How much more so when the government has found this unfortunate fact in the midst of its repeated declarations to protect industry? From the standpoint of those in the industry, at most, we can only sacrifice everything we have, abandon the efforts of decades, and throw it all away. Who will bear the heavy responsibility for the country's future production and the people's livelihood? Therefore, we must still ask the party and state authorities to weigh the pros and cons and investigate whether the telegram violates the spirit of the Provisional Constitution. At the same time, we also ask that it be corrected. We would be most fortunate for the future of industry. We send this telegram with great anxiety, awaiting your orders. Yong'an Textile Company, Sulun Yarn Factory, Minfeng Yarn Factory, Zhentai Yarn Factory, Baoxing Yarn Factory, Tianzhang Paper Factory, Dacheng Textile Factory, Hongzhang Textile Company, Dafeng Dyeing and Weaving Factory, Dalong Iron Factory, Guochang Enamelware Sales Office, Taishan Brick and Tile Company, Wuzhou Gubeng Factory, Wuhe Weaving Factory, Mei Ya Silk Weaving Factory, Zhanghua Woolen Textile Co., Ltd., Great China Match Co., Ltd., China Workers' Factory, China Ya'pu'er Electric Appliance Factory, Yixin Toothbrush Factory, China Enamel Factory, Yaguang Manufacturing Company, Huafu Hat Factory, Oriental Nianhong Electric Light Company, Lingsheng Ink Co., Ltd., Huasheng Electric Appliance Manufacturing Factory, Puyi Yarn Factory, Kaicheng Acid Manufacturing Factory, Kangyuan Factory, China Chemical Industry Society, Dasheng Yarn Factory, All Kowtow Sincerely.

According to Article 37 of the Provisional Constitution, the people have the freedom to engage in business. In law, this is an absolute private right and is not subject to public law. Now, the words in the telegram are not consistent with the provisions of the Provisional Constitution and deprive the people of their freedom to engage in business. China's industry is just beginning to sprout. It is subjected to the economic pressure of the great powers externally and the pain of natural disasters and man-made calamities internally.
