Fire Breaks Out Again at the Sanyou Factory Yesterday 33

▲ The Cause is Unknown, the Union Petitions for a Thorough Investigation

▲ The Capitalists Have Agreed to Issue the Ninth Installment of Food Allowances

According to Da Gong She, at 11:00 AM yesterday, a fire suddenly broke out in the white coal room of the Sanyou Industrial Society's main factory in Yinxiang Port. Thanks to timely rescue efforts, it did not become a major disaster. The cause of the fire is unknown. The union has submitted a petition to the party and government agencies, requesting a thorough investigation. In addition, at 4:00 PM, the factory's tap water suddenly stopped. The details are as follows:

▲ Another Fire Alarm: At 11:20 AM yesterday, a fire suddenly broke out in the factory's white coal room. For a time, thick smoke billowed and flames raged. Since no workers lived in the factory and the room was located on the barren ground at the back (adjacent to the woodworking room on the west and the ironworking room on the north), workers Zhang Dingliang and Wu Guocai discovered it. They rushed to the factory to investigate, but they were stopped by the security guard stationed at the factory gate. After negotiation, they were allowed to enter and quickly released the fire hose to put out the fire. They also notified the Yangshupu Fire Brigade and the Zhabei Second and Third Section Fire Brigades by telephone to rush to the scene. The fire was extinguished after twenty minutes. As a result, a section of the fence was burned, half a room was destroyed, and the loss of white coal, wood, and other items was relatively small. Afterwards, a reporter visited the factory to investigate and inquire about the cause of the fire. He met Shen Guocai, a worker stationed at the factory for security. According to him, the cause of the fire was quite peculiar, and it was difficult to know the truth. The coal room was located on the barren ground at the back, adjacent to the woodworking room on the west and the ironworking room on the north, and no one lived there, and no one ever came and went. It was very puzzling that a fire broke out. Fortunately, it was daytime and did not become a major disaster. If it had been at night, the consequences would have been unimaginable, he said.

▲ Petition for a Thorough Investigation: The Cotton Textile Industry Union of the Seventh District believes that the two fires at the factory are unusual. Yesterday, it specially submitted a petition to the party and government agencies, requesting a thorough investigation to clarify the truth. The original petition is as follows: "We are submitting a petition because a fire suddenly broke out at the Sanyou Society's main factory at around 11:00 AM today, at the location where the police detachment is stationed, requesting a prompt and thorough investigation to ensure public safety. Since the police detachment has been stationed at the factory since the 11th of this month, after the house near the factory on Mayushan Road was burned down on the morning of the 18th, an electrical fire occurred again two days later. The union has submitted written reports to the government and the bureau. Unexpectedly, at around 11:00 AM today, thick smoke suddenly billowed from the front section of the factory (i.e., the location where the police detachment is stationed). After the workers noticed it, they immediately requested to enter and inspect whether it was a fire in the factory. However, the members of the police detachment stopped them, refusing to allow them to enter. After repeated negotiations, workers Zhang Tingliang and Wu Guicheng were allowed to enter. When they traced the source of the smoke, they saw that the fire had started from the fence in the southeast corner of the small machine room and spread to the corner of the small machine room. At this time, the wind was very strong, and the danger was even greater. Therefore, the workers in the factory forced their way in and rushed to put out the fire. By the time the fire trucks from the concession arrived, the fire had almost been extinguished. It was found that the police detachment had completely removed the copper badges on their collars, making it impossible to identify them. This is suspicious point number one. When thick smoke billowed from the factory, they did not immediately investigate. This is suspicious point number two. When the workers noticed it, they requested to inspect it, but they still wanted to stop them. This is suspicious point number three. The area was not allowed for workers to enter and leave, and a fire suddenly broke out. This is suspicious point number four. Afterwards, when the crowd questioned them, they claimed not to know the reason. This is suspicious point number five. The police detachment bears the heavy responsibility of protecting the factory, but two fires have occurred in less than half a month. Not only did they not immediately investigate, but they also prevented the workers from putting out the fire. What is their intention? It is impossible to predict. Moreover, the front section of the factory is close to the Wangjiazhai Samsung Factory and the Shenjiazhai area on Mayushan Road. Fortunately, this incident occurred during the day, and it was discovered early. Fortunately, it was put out and did not cause a major disaster. If it had been late at night and there had not been enough time to rescue it, the harm would have been unimaginable. The union witnessed this with a heavy heart and could not sit idly by. Therefore, we have prepared a special document and submitted it to the government and the bureau, requesting a prompt and thorough investigation to protect public safety. We submit this urgently, awaiting your orders." Respectfully presented to the Municipal Government, Municipal Party Headquarters, Public Security Bureau, and Social Affairs Bureau.

▲ Chamber of Commerce's Reply: The Municipal Chamber of Commerce replied to the General Labor Union yesterday, saying: "We have received your letter of the 25th of this month, stating that the closure of the Yinxiang Factory of the Sanyou Society has caused a dispute. You have asked us to write to the factory manager to persuade him to reopen the factory as soon as possible and to discuss solutions. We have now received a notice from the Municipal Government that this matter has been submitted to arbitration. Therefore, how to resolve this matter fairly and justly is entirely within the scope of the arbitrators. We are sending this letter in reply, please take note." Respectfully to the Shanghai General Labor Union.

▲ Agreed to Provide Food Allowances: At around 10:00 AM yesterday, Zhu Guilin, a representative of the Social Affairs Bureau, Zhou Lianze, a representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, and Xia Zhongzhao and Gong Zitian, representatives of the labor union, went to the Sanyou Company to collect the food allowance for the ninth period. Wang Xianhua, the executive director of the company, received them and agreed to pay the full amount.

▲ Rescue Meeting: The Committee to Rescue the Starving Workers of the Sanyou Factory held a meeting yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM. The attending committee members were Zhou Xuexiang, Zhu Xuefan, Ye Xianggao, Shao Xubai, Chen Peide, and Zhao Zhenhui. Zhou Xuexiang chaired the meeting. Shao Xubai first reported on the process of persuading the workers to resume eating and resolved: (1) Confidential. (2) When the Municipal Government convenes the Arbitration Committee, representatives should be appointed to attend. It was resolved that Shao Xubai and Zhou Xuexiang should be appointed to attend. (3) A request should be submitted to the General Labor Union to order the labor unions to quickly raise donations for assistance. It was resolved that it should be passed.

▲ Water Supply Cut Off: At 4:00 PM yesterday, the water supply from all the faucets in the factory suddenly stopped. At that time, it was time for the workers to cook, so they panicked and rushed to report to the labor union. After receiving the report, the labor union immediately notified the British Shanghai Waterworks Company by telephone and inquired about the reason. According to the company, they did not send anyone to seal off the water supply. It was suddenly cut off, which was difficult to explain. They also said that since the person in charge of the company was not present, they could not send a craftsman to investigate, but they promised to try their best to restore it. However, as of the time the reporter submitted the manuscript, the water had not yet been restored.

Mr. Wang Luyi's Talk on the Dispute at the Dockworkers' Union 34

Recently, due to the dispute over the 28% system, the contractors saw that the central government's attitude was firm and ordered the municipal government to detain a small number of obstructive foremen. They then thought of using the excuse of improving the dockworkers' union first to divert attention. Yesterday, there was news that the municipal party headquarters was reorganizing the dockworkers' union. When the labor side heard the news, they were filled with righteous indignation and there was a tendency to strike, and the situation was deteriorating. Reporters visited the vice chairman of the Central People's Movement Committee and asked about the truth of the matter. His interview record is as follows: (Question) The dockworkers' 28% system problem has been delayed for four years, how will the central government resolve it? (Wang) The central government has made a very strong determination on this issue. However, to resolve the dispute, it is necessary to review the contractor's contract and find out how much the contractor's wage is. However, the contractor has repeatedly disobeyed orders. The central government has ordered the municipal government to enforce it and has telegraphed the municipal government to detain the obstructive foremen. This case can only be discussed after the contract is reviewed. (Question) It is recently heard that Mayor Wu will convene the directors of the Social Affairs Bureau and Public Security Bureau, as well as representatives of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Central Party Headquarters, and Ministry of Industry, this week to discuss the matter together. What is the main point of the discussion? (Wang) It is probably to discuss how to implement the central government's compulsory enforcement order and to discuss the implementation steps and methods for the 28% system in detail. (Question) It is heard that the Municipal Party Headquarters has reorganized the dockworkers' union yesterday, is it true? (Wang) I met Comrade Wu Kaixian a few days ago, and Wu mentioned it, but only said that he intends to improve the union committee. It is heard that the list of eleven people proposed by the Municipal Party Headquarters yesterday completely replaced the previous members of the union. Some of the members are even bank presidents and the largest contractors. The most surprising thing is that there are almost no workers among the members. This not only violates the six principles established by the central government, but also violates the central government's order that all unions must not be reorganized or established before the Trade Union Law is revised. I believe that reorganizing the dockworkers' union at this time will only make the situation more chaotic. Moreover, this matter is related to the livelihood of 80,000 dockworkers in Shanghai and the party's stance of supporting labor. I now want to send a letter to Comrade Wu to cancel this proposal. After finishing speaking, Committee Member Wang picked up a pen and wrote a letter to Wu, the general idea being that the dockworkers' union matter is of great importance, and the responsible comrades should deal with it carefully. It is heard that the members of the union include bank presidents and the largest contractors. This will only lead to more disputes, not only sacrificing the interests of labor, but also not helping the capitalists. It will only be the contractors who exploit from the middle who will receive the most blame. After finishing the letter, the reporter said goodbye and left.

Labor Dispute at Pudong Huachang Cured Radish Factory Resolved 35

▲ Seventeen Articles of Labor-Capital Contract Signed

According to Dagongshe, the workers of Pudong Huachang Cured Radish Factory went on strike on August 3 due to the factory's dismissal of female workers and demands for increased wages. The Social Affairs Bureau sent personnel to persuade them to return to work. The labor and capital sides signed a contract of seventeen articles at 6:00 PM the day before yesterday (the 26th), and representatives of the Municipal Party Headquarters, He Yuanming, and representatives of the Fifth District Party Headquarters, Zhang Yi, co-signed the contract. The labor dispute has been declared completely resolved. The original text of the contract is recorded below: (1) The factory recognizes the union's right to represent the union's workers. (2) The wages of the workers in the storage department will be increased by $2.50 from $7 to $8, $2.00 from $8 to $10, and $1.50 from $10 and above. The wages will be increased once every year thereafter. The workers will receive double wages in December. Other parts will receive bonuses as appropriate. (3) Workers who take sick leave will not have their wages deducted. The wages deducted from those who take leave for personal reasons will be distributed to the working workers. (4) Workers who encounter weddings or funerals may take two weeks of leave with pay. (5) Female workers who work for more than nine months will be given six weeks of leave with pay of 20 cents per day when they give birth. (6) The wages of the workers in the storage department will be paid as usual on the commemorative days stipulated by government laws and regulations. For other parts, male workers will receive 45 cents and female workers will receive 35 cents, which will be received by the union. (7) Workers who are injured on duty will have their medical expenses borne by the factory. (8) Workers who are injured or killed on duty will be given a compensation of $150 by the factory. (9) The factory will provide food and lodging for the workers in the storage department. (10) Supervisors and foremen must not abuse workers, arbitrarily deduct wages, and must not dismiss workers without reason. (11) The factory will subsidize the union with $20 per month, which will be received by the union. (12) (Drilling rod vehicles) Each drilling rod vehicle will be subsidized with one dime per day, and each cutting rod vehicle will be subsidized with seven cents per day. The factory will be responsible for carrying the baskets. (13) The tools for the drilling rod vehicles will be as usual. The tools for other parts will be paid at 70% of the current original price. (14) The cured radish parts will be calculated at 20 cents per 100 catties. (15) The radish slice parts will be increased by 17.5% per 10,000 slices according to the current price. (16) If there is a shortage of raw materials in each department, male workers will be subsidized with $8 for food and female workers will be subsidized with $6 per month, which will be paid every half month. (17) This contract will be implemented after being signed by both labor and capital. Factory representative, Huachang Cured Radish Factory Manager Shao Gaoxiang, Union representative, Executive Director Yan Quanrong, Shanghai Special Municipality Party Headquarters representative Hu Yuanming, Fifth District Party Headquarters representative Zhang Sheng.

City Chamber of Commerce Notice to All Sectors: Beware of Counterfeits 37

▲ Jiangyin Does Not Have a Dafeng Textile Mill

▲ The "Jiufeng" Trademark Is Fictitious

The City Chamber of Commerce, seeing that at a time when the promotion of national goods is enthusiastically advocated, there are always unscrupulous merchants who profit by counterfeiting, hindering the development of industry, has been diligently investigating. Recently, it was discovered that products bearing the "Jiufeng" trademark of the Dafeng Textile Mill in Jiangyin are being sold. Upon investigation, there is no such factory in Jiangyin at all. It can be known that it is counterfeit. Yesterday, a special notice was issued to all sectors to avoid being deceived. The original text is recorded below for the public scrutiny of national mass organizations:

The Chamber previously received reports that some people were altering Sichuan lingpai Zhigong ni and foreign yarn, etc., and changing them to the "Jiufeng" trademark of the Dafeng Textile Mill in Jiangyin to counterfeit national goods. It telegraphed the Jiangyin County Chamber of Commerce to investigate whether there was indeed a Dafeng Textile Mill there in order to handle the matter. It has now been reported back, relayed from the Fabric Industry Guild, that none of the guild's members, nor any other factories in the county, have this Dafeng brand. It is hoped that this will be carefully examined and investigated to protect national goods and warn unscrupulous merchants.

All national mass organizations and sectors are requested to pay attention. All Zhigong ni yarn and fabric using the "Jiufeng" trademark of the Dafeng Textile Mill in Jiangyin that are being sold in the territory are counterfeit goods and should be detained and investigated to prevent confusion.

Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce Respectfully.

City Chamber of Commerce Cables Government Requesting Negotiations on Fiji's Increased Egg Tax 38

The Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce yesterday telegraphed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Industry in Nanjing, saying:

Received a letter from the International Trade Bureau stating that, relayed from the Consulate General in Manila, the Fiji Legislative Council's Tax Department plans to increase the import tax on our country's eggs, ham, etc. The proposed increase in tax rates ranges from several times to twenty times. A memorandum is attached, requesting that all export merchants be notified to pay attention and find ways to prevent this. In addition to separately informing the relevant industries to pay attention, the case of negotiating the cancellation of the tax increase should still be handled by the Ministry instructing the consul stationed on the island to handle it locally.

Although increasing taxes is a right of each country, and it is not possible to protest through formal diplomatic channels, the silk merchants of that island can be informed of the mutual benefit of Sino-Fijian commerce, and it can be implicitly indicated that if Fiji increases taxes, our country should also increase the same taxes on the special products imported from that island into China to show opposition, so that they may have some scruples or a possibility of a change of heart. If a method of preventing this is set up here, Shanghai does not have a famous Fiji merchant doing business here, and the Americans also say that Fiji's internal affairs are autonomous and cannot be interfered with, and it is impossible to achieve the effect of national diplomacy. Therefore, we dare to report the facts as they are, and hope for consideration and action.

Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce Respectfully.

British Ship "Borxit" Confiscated 41

▲ Scheduled for Public Auction

The Dama Evening News reports that the British ship "Borxit" was confiscated by customs for smuggling 75 greyhounds into Shanghai. It is scheduled for public auction on September 16th. The ship was built in 1911 and was originally owned by a German merchant. It has a displacement of 1,658 tons, a length of 250 feet, a width of 38 feet, and a depth of 17 feet 9 inches. Later, it was purchased by the British company Enke Shi and flew the British flag. It arrived in Shanghai on August 9th.

Recent Status of Baoshan Seawall Project 42

The Baoshan seawall has been in disrepair for many years. After a major incident occurred in July of last year, the government and local gentry attached great importance to it. This year, the Jiangsu River Embankment Project Rehabilitation Committee allocated huge funds to carry out selective construction. The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Construction appointed Wan Kaijia as the director of the construction office. The construction site is divided into three sections: the first section is at Chenhua Beach in Shizilin, with a length of 189.5 zhang; the second section is at Niutoujing in Xuejia Beach, with a length of 420.0 zhang; and the third section is at Beiwang Temple in Zuowuyuedun, with a length of 150.0 zhang. The above still uses the old-style two-pile two-stone project. In addition, there are more than 330 zhang of cement seawall outer rock throwing projects. All kinds of materials used for wood and stone are purchased by the committee, and three inspectors are dispatched to supervise and accept the work at each construction section to show seriousness. In addition, the seawall embankment was previously dug for military trenches. This time, workers are also dispatched to tidy them up. All projects are scheduled to be completed before September 10th. Since construction started in mid-June, it has been in the dog days, and due to the tide, work is only done for half a day each day. Fortunately, the workers are working hard, and the staff and officers are also able to do their best. It is expected that it can be completed within the deadline.

Second Prison Public Notice: Parole Is Impartial 43

▲ Absolutely Not Obtainable Through Bribery and Solicitation

Xie Fuci, warden of the Jiangsu Shanghai Second Special Zone Prison, issued a notice yesterday, saying:

In the matter of this public notice, the handling of parole in this prison is impartial. All those who meet the parole regulations, have served two-thirds of their sentence, have good behavior in prison, and have evidence of remorse, will be applied for in stages according to the provisions of the law. It is absolutely not obtainable through bribery and solicitation. If any of the prison's staff or guards take the opportunity to spread rumors and deceive people, and dare to come and extort money, they can come to the prison to report them by name, or turn the person over to the nearby police or patrolman so that they can be punished according to the law. If the family members give fees privately and conceal the report, once discovered, in addition to immediately revoking the parole, those who have engaged in bribery will also be punished and will never be tolerated.

It is urgent to notify all family members in prison to be aware and not to be deceived, so as not to bring trouble on themselves. Important. This notice.

Case of Rioters Destroying Russian Newspaper Office 45

▲ Scheduled Pronouncement After Reopening Debate

On the evening of the 6th of this month, at 8:00 PM, several dozen rioters suddenly rushed to the Russian-language Shanghai Zhaila newspaper office at 551 Avenue Joffre in the French Concession, throwing stones and soda bottles, smashing the glass windows and other objects. Later, the detectives and Russian firefighters chased and captured Tang Xiangheng (a Jiangbei native who works as a rickshaw puller), Le Abang, and Lu Aqing (a coppersmith at the Huili Automobile Firm). After investigation by the police, they were found to be suspected of being reactionary and were sent to the Third Higher Branch Court for investigation. After a court hearing, Wang Shizong was designated as the lawyer to defend the defendants. The debate had originally concluded and a date was set for the pronouncement. However, due to the emergence of new evidence, the conclusion of the debate was revoked and the debate was reopened on record. The previous morning, Judge Lu, together with two judges, Guo and Fan, took the seat in the Third Criminal Tribunal to hear the case. Staff members of the Russian newspaper office were also brought to the court to conduct research. Because the case involved politics, by custom, onlookers were prohibited, and it was impossible to record the details of the interrogation. However, it was heard that the result was announced that

the debate was concluded and the pronouncement was scheduled for the 31st of this month.

Self-Help Society Widely Soliciting Members 48

The Chinese People's Livelihood Self-Help Society is dedicated to solving the social unemployment problem. It has a well-thought-out plan and complete organization. Since its preparation, it has been deeply praised by people from all walks of life. However, since the Shanghai war, all industries have been sluggish and materials have been difficult to obtain. Therefore, the society's fundraising has also been quite difficult. However, the number of unemployed people in society is increasing day by day, and various tragedies are intensifying. The society has the mission of providing relief to the unemployed, and it cannot ignore this. Therefore, it is now actively proceeding with widely soliciting members, not charging membership fees, but only requesting donations of one silver dollar as the society's start-up fund. The method of solicitation is that the society initiates a chain introduction to help people first, and a part of the city's Boy Scouts will volunteer to handle this chain introduction and collection procedures.

Madam Wei's Passing 50

▲ Funeral Procession This Morning

Madam Wei, the mother of Dr. Wei Daoming, the former Minister of Judicial Administration and Mayor of Nanjing, passed away at her Shanghai residence on June 23rd. The Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission telegraphed the Shanghai Municipal Government to send personnel to assist in the funeral. The funeral arrangements were divided into five groups: guidance, general affairs, documentation, ceremonies, and reception. The staff in each group included the director of the guidance group, Li Zhibo, the director of the general affairs group, Yang Zhaoxu, the director of the documentation group, Ma Shouhua, the director of the ceremonies group, Li Shuhua, and the director of the reception group, Zhu Luhe. When Madam Wei passed away, Dr. Wei was on a mission in Europe. Upon hearing the news, he rushed back to the country day and night. Yesterday (the 27th), he chose to set up a tent at the Yufosi Temple at the intersection of Gordon Road and Binlang Road to receive condolences. At 7:30 AM this morning, there was a family sacrifice. After 8:00 AM, Wu Tiecheng, the Mayor of Shanghai, represented Chairman Chiang Kai-shek of the Military Affairs Commission, Chu Minyi, the Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan, represented Premier Jiang of the Executive Yuan, Liu Yinglin represented the Ministry of Judicial Administration, and Luo Panhui represented the Shanghai Municipal Government to pay their respects.

The government agencies, groups, and schools that paid public tribute included the Northeast Branch of the Supreme Court, the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, the Third Branch of the High Court, the Shanghai First Special Zone Local Court, the Shanghai Second Special Zone Local Court, the Shanghai College of Political Science and Law, the World College, the Shanghai China Agricultural and Industrial Bank, and former Nanjing Municipal Government colleagues, etc. In addition, political and business figures such as Kong Xiangxi, Lin Xiang, Gao Lu, Wang Jingqi, Du Yuesheng, Zhang Xiaolin, Wang Xiaolai, Yu Qiaqing, Qian Xinzhi, Zhao Jinqing, Mu Ouchu, Wang Boqi, Xu Jilong, Jin Liren, Ye Zhuotang, French Minister and Consul Merry Aire, Chen Shiguang, Ji Hongchang, Liu Yufen, Xie Guansheng, Lin Biao, Wang Maoting, Lin Kanghou, etc. also came to express their condolences. Many elegiac couplets were received, such as Chiang Kai-shek's condolences: "The virtuous and capable dwell in the bamboo house, and the law officials of the capital have many merits." "The leaders are pushed forward in the Xuan, and the deer cart and gauze tent have a legacy." Lin Sen's condolences: "The husband's college is both Chinese and Western, and the skirt and cloth hairpins have facilitated the dream of studying abroad." "The talented children are both civil and military, and the Chinese toon family governs the country, all from the family's blessing." Ju Zheng's condolences: "The virtuous teachings are based on benevolence, and careful punishment is enough to match Ouyang's mother. The reputation overflows Zhanggong, and the biography should be compiled into Liu Xiang's book." Song Ziwen's condolences: "She has a distinguished vision and puts it into practice, and the family teachings have been upheld since she was a girl." "There are no millet fields in Qingmen, and Fu Sanxing." "The virtue and good deeds are about loving parents and encouraging children, and the family thrives in the white day." "The red pipe should be broadcast in Jiujiang." Zhang Xueliang's condolences: "The lotus pistil gives birth to fragrance, and the child's heart is infinitely bitter." "The daylily flowers wither suddenly, and the unexpected grief cannot be suppressed." It is said that the funeral procession will depart at 7:30 AM today (the 28th) with the participation of the concession police, the local court bailiffs, the public security bureau's infantry, pistol team, military band, and the garrison headquarters' military medicine team. Arrest of Kidnapping Suspects by the Public Security Bureau 51

Qiao Guanxiang's family, a carpenter residing at Daitieluqiao, Yingjing, west of the Hongqiao Road Airport in Xuhui District, was robbed on the 11th of this month at around 2:00 AM. The owner was beaten and injured, and his neighbor, Gu Yunting, was shot in both legs. Before leaving, Qiao's ten-year-old second son, Xiaoshun, was kidnapped and hidden, and a ransom was demanded in a letter. They agreed to contact them on the 24th, between 2:00 PM and 4:00 PM, west of the railway on Hongqiao Road in Xuhui District. After the owner reported to the Public Security Bureau and the Water Police, detectives disguised themselves and went to the scene. They arrested Song Wanjun and Ma Shifu, who were selling used goods, at the intersection of Yangzhai Road and Hongqiao Road. They were immediately sent to the first sub-bureau of the sixth district. The details have been reported previously. It is now learned that the contact point in this case is under the jurisdiction of the second sub-bureau of the sixth district. Chief Bi transferred all the witnesses to the second sub-bureau of the sixth district. After strict interrogation by Chief Liu, Song Wanjun confessed that he was 25 years old, from Rugao, and lived at No. 900 Fahua Town, and was engaged in the used goods business. Ma Shifu confessed that he was 29 years old, lived on Avenue Edward VII, and had been living with Song Wanjun, a fellow villager in the same industry, for three days. He denied the Qiao case. Chief Liu believed that the case was serious and yesterday prepared a document to send to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Kidnapping-Style Family Member Given a Light Punishment 52

▲ Poor Woman Subjected to Further Rape and Coercion

Yesterday at 6:40 PM, someone hired a car (Shanghai license No. 4235) and forcibly dragged a young woman onto the car at No. 15 Gongyi Lane, Xinmin Road, Zhabei. After she shouted for help, the police on duty at the scene stepped forward and arrested three people, including one woman and two men, as well as the car. They were all sent to the Fourth District Public Security Bureau. After interrogation by District Officer Zhu Ligong, the young woman claimed to be 22 years old, from Nanjing, and living at No. 15 Gongyi Lane, Xinmin Road. She was previously a prostitute. When she was 20 years old, she was sold by Su Qingyun, a friend of her brother-in-law, to Xu Delu, a family member at No. 133 Xinli Street, French Concession, to work as a prostitute. Because she could not stand the abuse, she escaped on April 26th of this year at 12:00 AM. On June 28th, she hired a lawyer to file a complaint with the court requesting to sever her relationship with Xu Delu and restore her freedom. Unexpectedly, at 5:00 PM today, while I was collecting clothes on the drying platform, I saw Xu and three or four companions arrive in a car. They shouted at me from below and forced me into the car. It looked like a kidnapping. Fortunately, after I shouted for help, the police officers of your district arrived and arrested three men and women. The rest had already fled. Although I have already escaped from Xu's place, my bill of sale is still with Xu Delu, so I do not want to file a lawsuit and request to be released for an out-of-court settlement, and so on. Xu Delu claimed to be 38 years old, from Yangzhou, living at No. 133 Dongxinli Street, Xinjie, French Concession, and running a brothel. Liu Guibao was sold to me by her brother-in-law through someone for 500 yuan silver dollars, with a term of four years. The term has not yet expired. When she ran away, I knew that Yang Boqing of Hui Pan Automobile Firm had taken her away, but I had no evidence to talk to him. I met Yang and negotiated with him on Datong Road, but he entrusted someone to come out and mediate, but there was no result. Now Liu Guibao can redeem herself, or she can still go back with me, and I will never force her. I request permission to go out for mediation, and so on. Another person, named Wang Aqing, 41 years old, from Ningbo, living at No. 139 Baker Road, Concession, drives a car for the Yellow Car Company and produced a driver's license. After District Officer Zhu verified the confession, because Liu Guibao had requested an out-of-court settlement, it should be approved. However, Xu Delu's behavior was out of the ordinary, so he was given a light punishment in accordance with the violation of police regulations. Wang Aqing was released without incident, and the car and car license were returned.

Verdict in Public Bus Fatal Accident 53

▲ Bus Driver Sentenced to Two Months Imprisonment

Liu Decai, a driver from Shandong of the Public Bus Company's No. 251 bus, drove No. 5031, Route 10 bus from south to north at 5:05 PM on the 25th of this month. Near Mugen Road and Wuding Road in Xuhui District, the driver carelessly knocked down Tao Genlong, who was riding a bicycle in front of him, crushing him to death. After investigation by the police, Liu was arrested and detained at the Xinzha Police Station, and Tao was sent to the Fellen Road Mortuary. The First Special Court dispatched Prosecutor Zhang Guangkui to the morgue to examine the body. It was found that the body of the body had been crushed to death. The report was confirmed. The driver, Liu Decai, was suspected of negligence in his duties, and it was ordered that he be immediately detained pending investigation and prosecution by the police. The details have been reported yesterday. It is now learned that the police have now prosecuted him for causing death by negligence in accordance with Article 291 of the Criminal Law. Yesterday morning, Liu Decai was brought to the Second Criminal Tribunal of the Special Court. The police lawyer, Wang Yaotang, gave a detailed account of the investigation, stating that at 5:05 PM on the 25th, the defendant was driving a public bus on Mugen Road near Wuding Road, heading north from the south. The deceased was riding a bicycle in front of him, also heading north from the south, driving on the west side of the road. The defendant honked the horn, hoping that he would avoid him, and at the same time veered to the east to avoid him. Unexpectedly, the deceased also veered to the east, causing the front wheel of the bus to hit the rear wheel of the deceased, causing him to fall to the ground and be crushed to death. Only witness Tang Rusheng witnessed the incident at the time. Tao was sent to Renji Hospital, but he had already died of serious injuries upon arrival. Yesterday, Prosecutor Zhang Chong verified the body and believed that the defendant was suspected of negligence and should be prosecuted by the police. However, according to the results of the investigation by the police, the defendant did not have any major suspicion, and the bus was traveling very slowly at the time. It was actually caused by the deceased's bicycle route being different, and so on. Witness Tang Rusheng also testified to everything. When questioned, the defendant, Liu Decai, testified that his car and the deceased's car were in the same direction, heading north from the south. I honked the horn three times, and the deceased looked back, but at that time the distance between the two cars was quite close. I quickly veered to the east to avoid him, but unexpectedly the deceased also veered to the east, causing him to collide, fall to the ground, and be crushed to death. He also hired lawyer Xu Shihao to defend him. After verification by Judge Wu Tingqi, Liu Decai was sentenced to two months of imprisonment for the crime of causing death by negligence in his duties.

Apprentice Swallows Saltpeter and Acid to Commit Suicide 54

Wu Huifu of Songjiang, residing at No. 8 Daji Lane, Wanyu Street, Nanshi, had a daughter, Abao, who was thirteen years old. Last year, he recruited Wu Renfu as his son-in-law. Renfu is eighteen years old this year. After entering the family, they have not yet married. Renfu has no job, so he was introduced to the National Printing Factory to study. It has only been two months. However, Wu Huifu's wife often complained because Renfu did not think about making progress. Renfu swallowed saltpeter and acid to commit suicide the day before yesterday. When he was discovered, he was immediately sent to Renji Hospital for treatment, but it was too late. He died yesterday. He was immediately sent home. The incident was learned by the First District Police Station, which ordered Lu Yongde, the local chief of the Sixteenth Pu, to report to the Local Court. Prosecutor Yang and others were commissioned to go to the scene to examine the body and confirmed that he died from poisoning. They instructed the family to collect the body and wait for further processing.

At the Jingyi Piano Factory established by Gu Zirong at No. 2 Shunwei Lane, Xinmin Road, Zhabei, around 3 PM the day before yesterday, a partner, Jiang Zhongfu from Ningbo, was moving wood when he carelessly caused the wood to fall. Warden of Xiamen Road Prison, Franklin, to Return Home 56

Mr. J.F. Pranklin, a British national and warden of the Xiamen Road Prison under the Shanghai Municipal Council, has served the council for over twenty-five years. He has made significant contributions to his duties. Five years ago, he received a long-service award from the council. He is known for his kindness and approachability and is highly regarded by his superiors. He also enjoys excellent relationships with the consular corps and legal circles, both Chinese and foreign. Having reached the end of his service and feeling tired and homesick, he has requested retirement from the council, which has reportedly been approved. He has received numerous letters of commendation from Sir Granville, the Shanghai British Assessor, Mr. Hsi Meng, the Dutch Consul in Shanghai, and Vice-Consul Fan Dengbao. It is also reported that Mr. Franklin will depart for his home country next month, first traveling to Honolulu and Canada for sightseeing.

Shanghai Four Banks Savings Society Hongkou Branch Moves into Self-Built New Building 57

The Hongkou Branch of the Shanghai Four Banks Savings Society has seen significant growth in its business, making the original rented premises insufficient. Therefore, it has purchased land south of Beisichuan Road and Bazilu to build a seven-story building with the latest type of safe deposit vault to provide convenient rental safe deposit boxes for residents of Hongkou at very low rates. It is reported that the branch will move into the new building tomorrow (29th) to conduct business.

Guanshengyuan, Old West Gate, Introduces New Sampan Porridge 58

Sampan porridge, a product of the boat dwellers of Guangzhou's Lychee Bay, is a type of assorted fish porridge known for its unique flavor and distinct style. Visitors to Lychee Bay invariably enjoy a bowl to savor its taste, and it is also called Lychee Porridge because of its origin. Chef Zhou, a renowned porridge maker from Lychee Bay, recently joined the culinary department of Guanshengyuan at the Old West Gate of Shanghai. He is showcasing his special skills at the store, offering the porridge for sale from 7:30 AM every morning. Priced at only twenty cents, those who have tried it are highly satisfied.

Canned Wuxi Wheat Gluten Arrives in Shanghai 59

Wuxi's special oil-fried wheat gluten is considered a supreme delicacy. Travelers to Wuxi often purchase it as a gift for relatives and friends. However, its oily nature makes it inconvenient to transport. The Sanle Agricultural Cooperative of Wuxi has specially produced canned wheat gluten. It was popular in Shanghai this summer, and with the Mid-Autumn Festival approaching, it is reported that the cooperative has sent a large batch to Shanghai to meet the demand for Mid-Autumn Festival gifts.

"Social Butterfly" Screening Today in Nanjing 60

The Fox Company's new film "Social Butterfly," starring heat-throb Jim Desmond, Pan McKee-Shallon, and Spear Pitcher, will premiere at the Nanjing Grand Theatre today. The film has received enthusiastic praise from European and American critics, who hail it as an unparalleled romantic masterpiece. Jim Desmond's expressions are considered to be at their peak, while Pan McKee-Shallon embodies the extravagance of a socialite. Spear Pitcher's internal portrayal is both profound and touching, creating a tragic yet passionate narrative.

Brothers Art Company Expands Enrollment 61

The Brothers Art Company, founded by artist Dong Qimeng, and its affiliated Shanghai Art Academy have seen enthusiastic enrollment from both male and female students due to their remarkable achievements. The academy offers two disciplines: Western painting and portrait painting, each with a dozen or so drawing techniques. Tuition fees are low, and success is rapid. Due to the increasing number of students from other locations, the academy has expanded the enrollment in its correspondence department from three hundred to five hundred students to facilitate greater access. Those interested can apply to the academy, enclosing four cents for postage to request a prospectus. The address is No. 653 Ningbo Road, Lloyd Road.

Soviet Gasoline Hits the Market 62

The gasoline market in Shanghai has traditionally been dominated by British and American merchants. However, it has been learned that since the Soviet Union decided to actively promote its products in China, it has established a sales agency in Shanghai on Guangdong Road called You Biandi Petroleum Company, abbreviated as U.R.T. in English. The company recently shipped a large quantity of Soviet gasoline and lubricating oil of excellent quality from the Batumi Oil Station in the Soviet Union on the Steven Wong. To facilitate user access, a gasoline pump has been set up at No. 607 Duoya Road, selling gasoline at one dollar and five cents per gallon. It has also been agreed with the Chinese Guanghua Petroleum Company to be the general distributor of Soviet gasoline. It is expected that there will be intense competition between the three types of gasoline - British, American, and Soviet - in the Shanghai market.

Minutes of the Meeting of the New Taikoo Dock Workers' Union 64

The New Taikoo Dock Workers' Union held a meeting of the organizing committee yesterday. Yang Mingwei was elected chairman. After a formal introduction and report on the significance of the meeting, the following items were discussed: (A) Regarding the reorganization of union affairs, it was proposed to elect eight members to be responsible for handling the matter. It was resolved that Yang Mingwei, Liao Zengxun, Wu Zichang, He Zhangming, Zhang Yin, Yan Baoyun, Ge Ren, and Shi Zhiqin be appointed as organizing committee members. (B) Shi Zhiqin proposed printing survey forms and distributing them to each branch and dock to be filled out and returned for statistical purposes. It was resolved to proceed actively with this. (C) Regarding how to handle the back dues owed by members of each branch before the Shanghai Incident, it was resolved to waive them all. (D) Regarding the collection of fees for reorganization, it was resolved that in addition to the existing membership fees, a reorganization fee of one yuan would be collected to facilitate development. (E) Regarding the lease of the union hall, it was resolved to entrust this to the administrative section. (F) In addition to notifying each branch, a declaration outlining the reorganization was to be drafted and distributed to each branch to clarify the situation. It was resolved to entrust this to the documentation section. (G) A motion was passed to appoint Comrade Zhao Huian as secretary of the union. The meeting then adjourned.

Supplement to the Shanghai News

Essays

Cremation 66

— A Buddhist

Yesterday's publication included an article by Mr. Zhang Tong discussing tomb improvements. Mr. Zhang's article was in response to Mr. Zhu Yunzong's article on tomb improvements. Mr. Zhang's point was that Mr. Zhu's advocacy of public cemeteries was not economical enough and advocated for cremation. I entirely agree with Mr. Zhang Tong's idea, but I do not fully endorse the methods he proposed. Although cremation is practiced in Japan and some places in the South Seas, I personally feel some unease and find it somewhat inhumane. This reminds me of an old joke:

A man was notoriously stingy and had three sons. As he was dying, he called his sons and asked them, "When I die, how will you handle the funeral arrangements?" The eldest son said, "I will provide fine clothes, a good coffin, and generous offerings." The man angrily said, "You unfilial son! You will ruin our family!" He then asked the second son. The second son said, "I will clothe you in alfalfa, put you in a reed mat, and bury you in the ground." The man said, "That's still too much trouble." Finally, he asked the youngest son. The youngest son said, "I will cut you up, salt you, and display you at the butcher's shop for those who want you." The man said, "That's an excellent method! But I have one request: Ask Uncle Er from next door not to buy on credit, as he has a terrible habit of not paying back!"

This joke scolds the typical miser and may seem overly harsh. However, there may be such stingy people in the world. Although this joke is unrelated to the advocacy of cremation, it shares a similar sense of stinginess and cruelty, so I have written it down here to amuse Mr. Zhang.

However, I have not yet found a satisfactory or reassuring solution to the system of tombs. I am naturally opposed to the old-style tombs, and I find that the current public cemeteries are somewhat aristocratic. We should still find a more economical solution.

Literature

Lament of a Deserted Wife 67

— Beard Farmer

When we first tied the knot, our love was immeasurably deep. Every morning, we exchanged sweet kisses, and every night, we shared the same bed. We hoped to grow old together, never counting the days until our hair turned white. But suddenly, a fierce storm of jealousy invaded, and my beauty withered day by day. I could not help but grieve in silence. My meddling sister-in-law, with her sharp tongue that could melt gold, caused my husband to listen to her biased words. My grievances sank to the bottom of the sea. Our love could not be salvaged, and I am now ashamed to be abandoned. I have gathered my dowry, but it is scattered and lost. Heartbroken, I bid farewell to the maids and painfully part with my sleeves. I want to embrace my pipa to leave, but I cannot find a confidant. Where can I go when I step out the door? I wipe away tears as they stream down my face. The man I served is no longer my husband; why should I still be attached? Late at night, as I think of the past, I long to shatter my Phoenix-seeking zither.

Science

An Experiment on the Leaning Tower of Pisa in the 20th Century 68

— Wang Zhaomei

| Exploring the Stratosphere |

What exactly is stratosphere exploration? And why was Professor Picard willing to risk his life for it on one occasion (May 27 of last year), a second (August 18), and a third? Most people, especially those who are not scientifically inclined, probably want to know. Please read this brief account:

The primary purpose of Picard's ascents was to measure the relationship between the intensity of "cosmic rays" and altitude. This is of immense value in physics, meteorology, and astronomy.

(2) Contributions to Physics. Among the newest issues in physics, the "mass-energy equivalence" theory can be considered the most important. The transformation of mercury into gold, the condensation of hydrogen into helium, and the possibility of harnessing atomic energy—such as the idea that one gram of energy could power a mail ship across the Pacific Ocean—have all arisen from this. Thus, if research in this area yields significant results, world civilization will inevitably progress from the "petroleum era" and "coal era" to the "electricity era" and finally the "atomic energy era." Around 1903, European physicists discovered radioactive matter. Later, they realized that there were highly penetrating light waves similar to X-rays existing on the surface. According to Milksan's experiments, this light wave was just as strong day and night, and it did not vary with the season. It could penetrate 57 meters of water and 5 meters of lead without any problem. Undoubtedly, it was considered a type of electromagnetic wave with a much shorter wavelength than X-rays. According to Einstein's theory of relativity's "mass-energy conversion formula," Milksan found that when hydrogen transforms into helium, the matter lost in this transformation can emit light waves of the same length as cosmic rays. How meaningful is this coincidence! Moreover, this light gradually absorbs and weakens as it penetrates the outer atmosphere of the earth. It can be seen that the high altitude (stratosphere) above six miles is a good experimental site, and its light intensity should vary with the distance from the ground. Picard's ascents were to find out whether this hypothesis was correct. The results of his experiments must provide new evidence for the "mass-energy interconversion theory." At the same time, the theory of relativity, which shocked the world, will also be proved or challenged by it.

(2) Contributions to Meteorology. In meteorology, especially in the study of atmospheric electricity, Professor Picard's experiments will have great significance. Various meteorological measurements in the stratosphere are one aspect, and the study of atmospheric electricity related to cosmic rays is another aspect. The air on the earth's surface has great insulation, but it also has considerable and measurable electrical conductivity, due to (1) the migration of electrons in oxygen molecules and gas molecules, i.e., the phenomenon of gas ionization, and (2) the effect of the earth containing radioactive substances. However, the combination of the above two is not enough to create the existing degree of ionization in the air, so Milkan believes that cosmic rays are the third cause. Professor Picard's research this time is on the nature of cosmic rays, so he has made some corrections and contributions in this regard.

(3) Contributions to Astronomy. The origin of celestial bodies, especially the origin of the solar system, is still a scientific mystery, and it can be said that it is as mysterious as the question of "the origin of life." Although there are three explanations—the nebula theory, the meteor theory, and the star cluster theory—each has its imperfections. First, let's talk about the sun. It is a hot mass of matter that constantly radiates energy to the earth and other planets. However, according to the shortest estimate of its lifespan, even if it is purely composed of radium, it should have died long ago. The only appropriate answer is the hypothesis of "energy-matter interconversion." Picard's ascents can prove the reliability of the energy-matter interconversion theory, and can also solve the problems of the sun and other celestial bodies. That is to say, whether this cosmic ray comes from the sun, or from a certain place in the universe, so we can use this new argument to further study the sun, or the origin of the sun.

In short, Picard does not want to live a monotonous life leading an annuity, but is willing to endure the cold and heat, and risk the unpredictable. His personal spirit should be admired, and the enthusiasm of the European people can also be praised. At the same time, the Shanghai press also pays great attention to this matter, with large headlines, and its phenomenon is also gratifying.

Society for the Improvement of Social Customs Discussion

Suggestion for Improving Wet Nurses 69

— Kang Shi

In middle- and upper-class families in our country, due to their wealth, they embrace the philosophy of enjoying life. Therefore, they mostly hire wet nurses to raise their children. However, these wet nurses are generally crude and uneducated, which inevitably leads to improper teaching, causing problems and endless troubles!

The teaching in childhood is the most important, because a person's character depends entirely on the nurturing in childhood. Appropriate parental teaching will produce good children, while inappropriate teaching will create bad children. It is like a factory; only with good machines can good products be produced!

I have seen many wealthy families who have hired wet nurses. However, in some cases, because the child's constitution and the wet nurse's constitution are incompatible, the child suffers from weakness and other diseases, which is extremely dangerous! Moreover, under the tutelage of uneducated wet nurses, of course, the child learns to be a young master, becoming decadent. This is not only a bad phenomenon for the family, but also a crisis for society. Therefore, I have written down the disadvantages of wet nurses and suggestions for improvement below. Are they appropriate? I would like to ask for your wise instructions!

1. Constitution: Everyone has their own constitution, with differences in heat and cold. In general, people who hire wet nurses only know that the wet nurse's body should be strong and the milk abundant, but they do not examine the constitution to see if it is suitable. Often, the wet nurse's body is very strong and the milk is very abundant, but the child is not fat or exceptionally thin, which is due to the incompatibility of the constitutions. Therefore, I think it should be improved. It is best not to hire a wet nurse, but to breastfeed yourself, because the constitution between mother and child is a natural connection. Do not sacrifice the child by embracing the philosophy of enjoying life! If that is not possible, you should take the wet nurse to a doctor to carefully examine whether she is suitable. In that case, there will be no unexpected accidents.

2. Teaching: In general, people who hire wet nurses hand over the child to the wet nurse, while they themselves spend their days in leisure. The wet nurse's care, of course, cannot be as attentive as one's own, and most wet nurses are uneducated. Their only principle is to listen to the child, because for the sake of livelihood, they cater to the owner's psychology in every way, not allowing the child's cries to be heard by the owner. Therefore, all the child's demands, toys, candy, etc., are provided to them, not daring to refuse in the slightest. This creates the child's arrogance and gradually fosters pride, and even the parents' orders are disobeyed. This is what the proverb calls the young master's temper! Therefore, I think it should be improved. The owners should often warn the wet nurses not to indulge the child's unreasonable demands, and should add strict rebuke. Moreover, they should not blame the wet nurse at random when they hear the child's cries. In that case, the child will not develop a young master's temper.

Alas!

A College Student 70

— Yi Ping

Mr. W is a college student. He has all the modern characteristics: a large amount of money, fashionable Western suits, but he considers it a lifelong regret that his parents gave him a less-than-perfect head and a not-so-beautiful face. However, he is determined to adhere to the motto of "Man can conquer nature" and "Buddhas need golden robes, and people need fine clothes," and strives to study cosmetology. Every Saturday and Sunday, he must sacrifice two hours for makeup. His drawer is like a one-stop shop in the French Concession, with razors, Hazelene, Babyface, Stendhal, White Medicine God, wooden combs... even more than the KissProof that women put in their handbags when they go out. He also frankly crosses the line to build roads, preparing everything for great use.

But heaven is not merciful. No matter what, he has never seen a modern girl on his arm.

So he retreated to the second-best option. As long as he sees the words "Ms. XXX, talented student from X Girls' School" in a picture magazine or somewhere, he ignores the consequences and writes sickeningly sweet love letters one after another, until he himself feels embarrassed, and then looks for another target. But his work is like a long-term resistance, with zero effect.

Finally, he had a wild idea and wrote erotic poems in a trivial tabloid. He wanted to use this to flatter the girl of his dreams and make her favor him, saying things like "Adorable woman! You are charming and sensual, you have a fair face, you have blood-red lips, high breasts, and thick thighs, all of which are symbols of your fitness. Ah! Adorable woman, you also feel the boredom of sex." For a time, the slogan of "sex maniac" caused many future female scholars to jointly request the principal to expel him. A piece of paper with the verdict came down, approving the request.

On the night of his departure, he hosted a banquet for many classmates. At the banquet, he unexpectedly gave a generous and passionate speech. "Everyone, I am heartbroken that China's demise is imminent, and those in power have no way to deal with it. What's the use of studying? So I pursue women to temporarily numb my nerves. You must know how painful it is to be a slave of a conquered country! Now..." He raised a big fist and waved it in the air, just like a military officer delivering a speech to kill the enemy. "My dream is awake! Today is our last time together. I am going to the Northeast to join the Volunteer Army, fight for the cause, and die for the nation. Everyone, who is willing to join, raise your hand!" But only his fist was seen extending and retracting in the air.

A week later, his name was found again in a certain wild chicken university, and his erotic poems were still published in a certain tabloid. There was a pair of small pliers and a box of foreign-lettered things in the drawer of his drawer, more makeup products.

Incurable.

A Glimpse of a Training Session 71

— Jin

August X to August XX, this is when the XX County XX training session was held. The meeting place was in XX, the location was very suitable, and the transportation was very convenient. Although the training time was only fifteen days, several jokes happened in these short fifteen days. They are excerpted as follows:

(1) Some members have a listening sickness. The purpose of their coming is to eat, because they are provided with food and accommodation, so they are very casual about listening to the lectures. After hearing the bell, several members lie down comfortably in bed, this one saying he has a headache, that one saying he has a stomachache, and he also says he has heatstroke, making the host helpless. After the lectures are finished, their illnesses slowly get better, especially when it comes to eating, they still have to eat three or four bowls even though they are sick?

(2) Truancy The members of the XX training session are all elementary school teachers. The young ones are in their twenties, and the old ones are in their forties and fifties, and the lecturers are also very young. In contrast, they can't help but feel ashamed, [this may be my guess] so everyone sneaks out one by one halfway through the lecture. This is a common fact.

(3) Female Comrades One day, several female comrades came from XX. Their faces were the color of goose eggs, their bodies were slender, and their clothes were modern. Suddenly, they attracted the attention of most of the members of the meeting. These female comrades also considered it an honor to listen to an hour of lectures. For this hour, the manpower was very grand, and even the friends who had a listening sickness were cured. But what is the purpose of their listening to the lectures?

Alas! This is the outline of the XX training session.

Degeneration

The Life of a Modern Woman 72

— Jinlong

I have a girlfriend, "She is a graduate of XX Junior High School. It has been nearly two years since she and I separated. Yesterday, I happened to meet her on the so-called mysterious street. In a conversation, I learned that she is working as a mysterious masseuse in XX Massage Parlor on Bazilu.

I said; "Li! Long time no see, how are you?"

She said, "It's embarrassing to say, since I graduated from XX school, because my old father passed away, I can't continue my studies and I can't find a suitable job for a while. To be honest, I'm really ashamed, I'm working as a masseuse in XX Massage Parlor now!"

"Oh! Masseuse" When I heard the word masseuse, I felt strangely uncomfortable in my heart. In my ideal, a massage parlor is a very mysterious den, maybe it is a disguised:::

She said, "I have degenerated! But I can't care about shame, you know that there is only my only loving mother in my family, I have to maintain the life of mother and daughter, and I have to do those lowly tasks, you have to forgive my difficulties,"

I said, "Then how much is your monthly salary there?"

She said, "It's very pitiful, not only do I have no salary, but I also have no share of the commission. All the benefits are taken by the parlor owner. The life of the masseuses depends entirely on the rewards of the customers. As for the price of the rewards, I don't want to say."

After she finished speaking, she couldn't help but shed ashamed and great hot tears, and I also shed tears of sympathy for her, and I parted with her in sorrow, Ah! Masseuse. Poor masseuse!

The appellee shall compensate the appellant silver 992 taels, of which 250 taels shall accrue annual interest of 5% from November 1, year 20; 724 taels shall accrue annual interest of 5% from December 1, year 20; and 16 taels shall accrue annual interest of 5% from January 1, year 21, until the date of execution. The litigation costs of the first and second instances shall be borne by the appellee.

▲ One appeal case of Zhou Xuehai versus Yuan Moqin involving a divorce dispute. (Ruling) The appeal is rejected. The litigation costs of the second instance shall be borne by the appellant.

▲ One retrial case of Minsheng Paper Mill versus Tianli Foreign Firm involving damage compensation for machinery and payment for goods. (Ruling) The appeal is rejected. The litigation costs of the second and previous third instances shall be borne by the appellant.

▲ One appeal case of Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank versus Davis involving compensation dispute. (Ruling) The original judgment is altered. The appellee's claim is rejected. The litigation costs of the first and second instances shall be borne by the appellee. (Above are dated August 26th)

▲ Criminal Judgment: One case of Zhang Afu involving robbery. (Ruling) The appeal is rejected.

▲ One case of Ma Ciqing involving counterfeiting postage stamps. (Ruling) The original judgment concerning Ma Ciqing is revoked. Ma Ciqing is sentenced to six months imprisonment and fined 200 yuan for using postage stamps with defaced cancellation marks. If the fine is not paid in full, one day of imprisonment will be substituted for every two yuan. The number of days of pre-trial detention will be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. The postage stamps with defaced cancellation marks are confiscated.

▲ One case of Wu Chenshi, et al. involving kidnapping for profit. (Ruling) The original judgment concerning Wu Chenshi, Chen Niushi, and Zhou Aniang is revoked. Wu Chenshi, Chen Niushi, and Zhou Aniang are each sentenced to six years imprisonment for continuous joint intention to kidnap men and women under the age of twenty for profit, thereby causing them to leave the persons with parental rights. The number of days of pre-trial detention will be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment.

▲ One case of Chen Alin involving theft and fraud. (Ruling) The appeal is rejected.

▲ One case of Zhang Jinsheng involving attempted intimidation. (Ruling) The appeal is rejected.

▲ One case of Tan Yuelan, et al. involving opium. (Ruling) The appeal is rejected.

▲ One appeal case of Chen Xinzhai involving obstruction of public morals. (Ruling) The appeal is rejected. (Above are dated August 26th)

▲ Criminal Judgment: Huishan Police Station sues Zhou Taixing, et al., for opium-related charges. (Ruling) Zhou Taixing is sentenced to six months imprisonment and fined sixty yuan for providing premises for opium smoking with the intention of profit. Wang Laiquan, Hai Bao, Zhang Tuzi, and Xu Guogan, as repeat offenders of opium smoking, are each sentenced to two months imprisonment and fined forty yuan. Gao Ziqiao, Qiao Xiaogouzi, and Wang Lianqing are each sentenced to one month imprisonment and fined twenty yuan for opium smoking. If the fines are not paid through compulsory execution, one day of imprisonment will be substituted for every two yuan.

The number of days of pre-trial detention will be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. The opium paraphernalia, etc., are confiscated as per the list.

▲ Hongkou Police Station sues Wang Asi for theft. (Ruling) Wang Asi, as a repeat offender of theft, is sentenced to three months imprisonment. The number of days of pre-trial detention will be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment.

Xu Shansheng, Xue Zhongyuan, He Zhufu, Zhou Afu, and Wang Wangshi are each sentenced to a reduced term of one month imprisonment and fined thirty yuan for opium smoking. Shanghai Second Special District Local Court 77

▲ Criminal Judgment: Police Department v. Zhao Bingtu et al., Case of Military Firearms (Main Text) Yang Caoshi is sentenced to eight months imprisonment for possessing military pistols and bullets without permission and for failing to prove a legitimate reason. The number of days of pre-trial detention shall be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days for each day of imprisonment. One pistol and four bullets are confiscated. Zhao Bingtu is found not guilty.

▲ Police Department v. Guo Haishan et al., Case of Theft and Stolen Goods (Main Text) Guo Haishan is sentenced to two years imprisonment for the crime of joint theft. Guo Xushi is sentenced to three months imprisonment for the crime of joint theft. The number of days of pre-trial detention shall be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days for each day of imprisonment. Guo Xushi is granted a two-year suspended sentence. Wang Jianxiu, Xia Wen, Wu Ruiliang, and Chen Dezhang are all found not guilty.

▲ Police Department v. Shen Tanru et al., Case of Opium (Main Text) Shen Tanru is sentenced to six months imprisonment and fined one hundred yuan for providing premises for opium smoking with the intention of profit. Jiang Guanrong and Wang Rongzhou are each sentenced to one month imprisonment for the crime of opium smoking. If the fine is not paid, one yuan will be converted to one day of imprisonment. The number of days of pre-trial detention shall be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days for each day of imprisonment. Jiang Guanrong and Wang Rongzhou are granted a three-year suspended sentence. Opium paraphernalia, opium pipes, etc., are confiscated as per the list.

▲ Police Department v. Tang Bingkai et al., Case of Opium (Main Text) Tang Bingkai is sentenced to six months imprisonment for providing premises for smoking opium substitutes with the intention of profit. Zhang Amao is sentenced to two months imprisonment for the crime of smoking opium substitutes as a repeat offender. Pan Shiqing, Yang Asi, Ni Afu, and Hu Wangshi are each sentenced to one month imprisonment for the crime of smoking opium substitutes. The number of days of pre-trial detention shall be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days for each day of imprisonment. Pan Shiqing, Ni Afu, and Hu Wangshi are granted a three-year suspended sentence. Opium paraphernalia, red pills are confiscated as per the list.

▲ Civil Judgment: Lin Houfu v. Zhang Xitang et al., Case of Vehicle Fare (Main Text) The defendant Zhang Xitang shall repay the plaintiff 1,740 yuan. If the compulsory execution on Zhang Xitang's assets is ineffective, the defendants Gui Liang and Zhang Gengshan shall bear joint and several liability for the repayment. Litigation costs shall be borne by the defendants.

▲ Jin Yuan Company and Xia Guoliang v. Jia Hanqi et al., Case of Rent Arrears (Main Text) Jia Hanqi shall repay the plaintiff 288 yuan and terminate the lease agreement. Xu Guitang shall repay the plaintiff 107.6 yuan plus 0.2 small yuan. Litigation costs shall be borne by Jia Hanqi for three-quarters and Xu Guitang for one-quarter.

▲ Zhou Bolin v. Aidu Inn and Li Linfa, Case of Debt (Main Text) The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 2,000 yuan, with interest calculated at an annual rate of 2% from the fourth day of the eighth lunar month of the 18th year of the Republic of China until the date of execution, calculated according to the Gregorian calendar. The plaintiff's remaining claims are rejected. Litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲ Ruling on a Case: Peng Buyu, as the shop owner, requests direct execution against the debtor Jiang Huanzhang, who has left Shanghai. The court has reviewed the petition and found that the debtor, Xue Chongxing, who is from Jiaxing, voluntarily surrendered and guaranteed to clear the debt within a specified period. Now that Xue Chongxing has failed to pay the debt by the deadline, Jiang Huanzhang should be held liable to pay on his behalf. The petition claiming that Jiang Huanzhang's departure from Shanghai is intended to relieve him of responsibility is inappropriate. Therefore, this petition is rejected.

▲ Criminal Judgments

Verdict in the Chen Wenbiao theft case: (Main text) Chen Wenbiao is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for stealing at the train station. Days detained before the verdict is finalized will be converted at a rate of two days of detention for one day of imprisonment.

Verdict in the Li Pinhua disrupting a family case: (Main text) Li Pinhua is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for enticing a woman under the age of twenty away from the person with parental authority. Days detained before the verdict is finalized will be converted at a rate of two days of detention for one day of imprisonment.

Verdict in the Wang Zilin opium case: (Main text) Wang Zilin is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for possessing opium with the intention of selling it and is also fined 150 yuan. If the fine is not paid through compulsory execution, it will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of one yuan per day. Days detained before the verdict is finalized will be converted at a rate of two days of detention for one day of imprisonment. One package of opium weighing 31 taels is confiscated.

Verdict in the Yang Baoqing opium case: (Main text) Yang Baoqing is sentenced to one year and two months of imprisonment for possessing opium substitutes with the intention of selling them and is also fined 150 yuan. If the fine is not paid through compulsory execution, it will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of one yuan for every two days. Days detained before the verdict is finalized will be converted at a rate of two days of detention for one day of imprisonment. One package of morphine weighing 13.5 taels is confiscated. (Above dated August 25th)

(Main text) One opium pipe, one lamp stand, and forty red pills are confiscated.

▲ Verdict in the Zhang Li Shi opium case

(Main text) Zhang Li Shi is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for possessing opium with the intention of selling it and is also fined 150 yuan. If the fine is not paid through compulsory execution, it will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of one yuan per day. Days detained before the verdict is finalized will be converted at a rate of two days of detention for one day of imprisonment. Seventy-six taels of opium are confiscated.

▲ Verdict in the Zhu Wang Shi opium case

(Main text) Zhu Wang Shi is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for possessing opium with the intention of selling it. Days detained before the verdict is finalized will be converted at a rate of two days of detention for one day of imprisonment. Thirty-six taels of opium are confiscated.

▲ Verdict in the Lu Lin Shi disruption of family case

(Main text) Lu Lin Shi is sentenced to ten months of imprisonment for each of the two crimes of jointly and intentionally enticing a man under the age of twenty away from the person with parental authority for profit, with a fixed term of imprisonment of one year and two months. Days detained before the verdict is finalized will be converted at a rate of two days of detention for one day of imprisonment.

Verdict in the Xu Xiamin escape case

(Main text) Xu Xiamin is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for causing the escape of a person lawfully arrested due to negligence. Days detained before the verdict is finalized will be converted at a rate of two days of detention for one day of imprisonment.

Verdict in the You Zhide and others opium case

(Main text) Ju Zhide is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for providing a premises for others to smoke opium substitutes and is also fined 60 yuan. If the fine is not paid through compulsory execution, it will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of one yuan per day. Days detained before the verdict is finalized will be converted at a rate of two days of detention for one day of imprisonment. Qin Qiansong, Qin Wanqing, Jiang Maochang, and Wang Jizi are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment for using opium substitutes and are also fined 20 yuan. If the fine is not paid through compulsory execution, it will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of one yuan per day. Days detained before the verdict is finalized will be converted at a rate of two days of detention for one day of imprisonment. Six opium pipes, seven lamps, one opium tray, two opium picks, two pairs of tongs, eighty red pills, and a small amount of opium ash are confiscated. (Above dated August 25th)

▲ Civil Judgment

One judgment in the case of Fugui Ji v. Zhao Jieting regarding debt. (Main text) The defendant shall repay the plaintiff's loan of 300 taels of silver, plus annual interest of 5% from March 1, 1929, until the date of execution. The cost of litigation shall be borne by the defendant. Defendant Zhao Jieting is hereby notified by public notice. (The full text is posted and announced in this court.)

Public Notice Served: The full text is posted and announced in this court.

One case of Huang Fu v. Qian Gengsheng and others regarding a rent case.

▲This court has scheduled a public hearing for 9:00 AM on September 16th. Said defendant is required to appear in court on time for arguments and must not delay or cause yourself harm. Defendant Qian Gengsheng and Cai Erlang are hereby notified by public notice.

▲Public Notice Served: (The full text is posted and announced in this court.)

▲ One judgment in the case of Peng Xueying v. Cai Yimin regarding dissolution of engagement. (Main text) The plaintiff's claim is dismissed, and the costs of both parties shall be borne by the plaintiff. Defendant Cai Yimin is hereby notified.

▲Criminal Rulings:

Guo Liu Shi's withdrawal petition is acknowledged. This ruling.

Zhang Qixiu's request for prompt investigation and accompanying civil lawsuit is acknowledged. The case has already been dismissed and the police have been instructed to deliver it. The Zhang Chen Shi refused to accept it on file. The petitioner shall wait for it to be delivered again. This ruling.

Zhou Quanshou's petition is acknowledged. Further action will be taken after the defendant is apprehended. This ruling.

Wang Xingzhao's preliminary statement is acknowledged. A further petition for verification shall be submitted after the whereabouts of your wife are ascertained. This ruling.

Cai Huaiqing's petition for filing is acknowledged. If the civilian woman was indeed abducted, legal action should be taken. The petitioner shall come to the court to file a complaint. This ruling.

Li Zhu Shi's rape case petition is acknowledged. The Public Security Bureau should await legal action. The petitioner shall be notified. (Above dated August 26th)
